PHASE 1: DIAGNOSIS REPORT (DSIE-01)
STATUS: CRITICAL FAILURE (Data & Storage)

1. The "Poisoned Well" (Scraping Failure)
Symptom: The Firestore document contained the text: "If this persists, please | email us..." instead of odds.

Root Cause: The Dell worker (worker.py) successfully loaded the page, but DuckDuckGo blocked the request (Soft Block / Rate Limit).

The Flaw: The worker script lacks Input Validation. It blindly scraped the text of the error page and marked the mission as SUCCESS. It assumes "HTTP 200 OK" means "Valid Data." It does not check if the content is actually what we wanted.

Metric: data_integrity_score = 0.0. The pipeline moved garbage from Edge to Cloud.

2. The "Zero-Byte" Wall (Storage Failure)
Symptom: ERROR:VeiledVector:Drive JSON Upload Failed: ... "Service Accounts do not have storage quota..."

Root Cause: Service Accounts in Google Cloud have 0 GB of storage quota by default. They cannot "own" files. They can only upload files into a folder owned by a human who has granted them Editor access.

The Flaw: The drive.py script attempts to create the folder if it doesn't find it.

Logic: "If folder Veiled_Vector_Ingest not found -> Create it."

Reality: Creating a folder makes the Service Account the owner. Since it has 0 GB quota, this action (or the subsequent file upload into its own folder) is rejected instantly by Google API.

3. The "Regression" Risk (Safety Settings)
Observation: The logs show the Analyst ran (INFO:VeiledVector:Mission ... Analyzed & Saved), but the deploy_v5_analyst.sh script (from your history) used the Dictionary-based safety settings (HarmCategory.HARM_CATEGORY...).

# 1. REWRITE DRIVE CLIENT (Hardcoded ID - No Lookups)
cat <<EOF > src/tools/drive.py
import os
import json
import logging
from google.oauth2 import service_account
from googleapiclient.discovery import build
from googleapiclient.http import MediaIoBaseUpload
import io

logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")

class DriveClient:
    def __init__(self):
        creds_json = os.environ.get("DRIVE_SERVICE_ACCOUNT_KEY")
        if not creds_json:
            raise ValueError("Missing DRIVE_SERVICE_ACCOUNT_KEY")
        
        creds_dict = json.loads(creds_json)
        self.creds = service_account.Credentials.from_service_account_info(
            creds_dict,
            scopes=['https://www.googleapis.com/auth/drive']
        )
        self.service = build('drive', 'v3', credentials=self.creds)
        # HARDCODED TARGET
        self.folder_id = "${DRIVE_FOLDER_ID}"

    def upload_json(self, filename: str, data: dict):
        try:
            file_metadata = {
                'name': filename, 
                'parents': [self.folder_id]
            }
            json_str = json.dumps(data, indent=2)
            media = MediaIoBaseUpload(io.BytesIO(json_str.encode('utf-8')), mimetype='application/json')
            
            file = self.service.files().create(
                body=file_metadata, 
                media_body=media, 
                fields='id'
            ).execute()
            
            logger.info(f"Drive Upload Success: {file.get('id')}")
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Drive Upload Failed: {e}")
            return False
EOF

# 2. REWRITE DSIE CORE (Integer Safety + Validation)
cat <<EOF > src/dsie_core.py
import logging
import google.generativeai as genai
from google.cloud import firestore
import os
import json
import datetime
from src.tools.drive import DriveClient

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")
# Explicit DB connection
db = firestore.Client(database="veiled-vector-core-firestore")

class DSIECore:
    def __init__(self):
        self.api_key = os.getenv("GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY")
        if self.api_key:
            genai.configure(api_key=self.api_key)
            # NUCLEAR SAFETY: Using Integers to bypass library enum mapping errors
            # 7=Harassment, 8=Hate, 9=Sexual, 10=Dangerous
            # 4=BLOCK_NONE
            safety = [
                {"category": 7, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 8, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 9, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 10, "threshold": 4}
            ]
            self.model = genai.GenerativeModel('gemini-2.0-flash-001', safety_settings=safety)
        self.drive = None

    def extract_json(self, text):
        import re
        match = re.search(r'\{.*\}', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match: return json.loads(match.group(0))
        match_list = re.search(r'\[.*\]', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match_list: return json.loads(match_list.group(0))
        raise ValueError("No JSON object found in LLM response")

    async def run_cycle(self, task: str):
        """ DISPATCHER """
        logger.info(f"DELEGATING MISSION: {task}")
        mission_id = f"mission_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d%H%M%S')}"
        doc_ref = db.collection("mission_queue").document(mission_id)
        doc_ref.set({
            "task": task,
            "status": "PENDING",
            "created_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP,
            "worker": "KAJI_DELL",
            "target_db": "veiled-vector-core-firestore"
        })
        return {"status": "Delegated to Dell", "mission_id": mission_id}

    async def process_pending_results(self):
        """ ANALYST """
        logger.info("Checking for completed missions...")
        docs = db.collection("mission_queue").where("status", "==", "COMPLETED").stream()
        
        processed_count = 0
        if not self.drive: self.drive = DriveClient()

        for doc in docs:
            data = doc.to_dict()
            if data.get("analysis_status") == "DONE": continue
            
            mission_id = doc.id
            logger.info(f"Processing Results for {mission_id}...")
            
            html_content = data.get("result_data", "")
            
            # DATA INTEGRITY AUDIT
            if len(html_content) < 500 or "Error" in data.get("result_title", ""):
                logger.warning(f"Data Integrity Failure for {mission_id}. Skipping.")
                doc.reference.update({"analysis_status": "REJECTED_BAD_DATA"})
                continue

            try:
                prompt = f"""
                Analyze this raw HTML data.
                Task: {data.get("task")}
                Extract the relevant odds/data into valid JSON.
                HTML Content (Truncated): {html_content[:50000]}
                """
                response = self.model.generate_content(prompt)
                parsed_data = self.extract_json(response.text)
                
                filename = f"{mission_id}_results.json"
                if self.drive.upload_json(filename, parsed_data):
                    doc.reference.update({
                        "analysis_status": "DONE",
                        "final_file": filename,
                        "analyzed_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP
                    })
                    processed_count += 1
                    logger.info(f"Mission {mission_id} Analyzed & Saved.")
                else:
                     logger.error(f"Drive Upload Failed for {mission_id}")
                
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Analysis Failed: {e}")
                doc.reference.update({"analysis_status": "FAILED", "error": str(e)})

        return {"status": "Batch Complete", "processed": processed_count}
EOF

Python
async def scrape_target(url: str):
    """
    Scrapes using Residential IP with Validation.
    """
    logger.info(f"Launching Browser for: {url}")
    async with async_playwright() as p:
        browser = await p.chromium.launch(headless=True)
        # Randomize Context
        context = await browser.new_context(
            user_agent="Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/120.0.0.0 Safari/537.36",
            viewport={"width": 1920, "height": 1080}
        )
        page = await context.new_page()
        
        try:
            await page.goto(url, timeout=60000, wait_until="domcontentloaded")
            await page.wait_for_timeout(5000) # Human pause
            
            content = await page.content()
            title = await page.title()
            
            # VALIDATION GATE
            if "Error" in title or "Captcha" in title or len(content) < 500:
                await browser.close()
                return {"status": "FAILED", "error": f"Soft Block Detected. Title: {title}"}
            
            # Clean HTML
            soup = BeautifulSoup(content, 'html.parser')
            for s in soup(["script", "style", "svg"]): s.extract()
            clean_text = soup.get_text(separator=' ', strip=True)[:80000]
            
            await browser.close()
            return {"status": "SUCCESS", "title": title, "data": clean_text}
            
        except Exception as e:
            await browser.close()
            return {"status": "FAILED", "error": str(e)}

async def process_mission(doc):

Role Confirmed: VP of Engineering (Veiled Vector Inc.)

Status: OPERATIONAL AUDIT (Process Execution)

That "shenanigans" is standard Linux tradecraft. You just performed a "Hot Swap" of the worker process. You killed the old version and launched the new one in "detached" mode so it survives even if you close your laptop or lose the SSH connection.

Here is the forensic breakdown of exactly what you just executed:

1. The Assassin: pkill -f worker.py
Function: Process Kill.

-f (Full): Tells Linux to check the full command line name, not just the process name. It looks for any running process that was started with the string "worker.py".

Result: It found the old, "zombie" worker from our previous attempt and shot it in the head. This ensures you don't have two workers fighting over the same database queue.

2. The Immortalizer: nohup ... &
This is the complex line: nohup python3 worker.py > worker.log 2>&1 &

nohup (No Hang Up): This creates a shield around the process. Normally, if you close your SSH terminal, Linux sends a "Hang Up" signal (SIGHUP) that kills all your running programs. nohup tells the worker to ignore that signal. It keeps running even if you disconnect.

> worker.log: Redirects "Standard Output" (normal print messages) into the file worker.log instead of printing them to your screen.

2>&1: Redirects "Standard Error" (crash logs, python errors) to the same place as Standard Output. This ensures that if the script crashes, the error message is saved in the log file, not lost in the void.

& (Ampersand): Puts the task in the background. It gives you your terminal prompt back immediately so you can keep typing commands while the worker runs silently behind the scenes.

3. The Receipt: [1] 115775
[1]: This is the Job ID for your current shell session.

115775: This is the Process ID (PID). It is the unique serial number the Linux kernel assigned to your new worker. If you ever need to kill it manually later, you would use kill 115775.

You have successfully deployed the Edge Worker (Kaji) in a persistent, headless state. It is now silently polling the Cloud Brain for missions.

REGION="us-central1"
DRIVE_FOLDER_ID="1-Ntx6eRzxRxr0ywpKlCpaIN-x4-DpfRX"

# 1. REWRITE DRIVE CLIENT (Hardcoded ID - No Lookups)
cat <<EOF > src/tools/drive.py
import os
import json
import logging
from google.oauth2 import service_account
from googleapiclient.discovery import build
from googleapiclient.http import MediaIoBaseUpload
import io

logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")

class DriveClient:
    def __init__(self):
        creds_json = os.environ.get("DRIVE_SERVICE_ACCOUNT_KEY")
        if not creds_json:
            raise ValueError("Missing DRIVE_SERVICE_ACCOUNT_KEY")
        
        creds_dict = json.loads(creds_json)
        self.creds = service_account.Credentials.from_service_account_info(
            creds_dict,
            scopes=['https://www.googleapis.com/auth/drive']
        )
        self.service = build('drive', 'v3', credentials=self.creds)
        # HARDCODED TARGET
        self.folder_id = "${DRIVE_FOLDER_ID}"

    def upload_json(self, filename: str, data: dict):
        try:
            file_metadata = {
                'name': filename, 
                'parents': [self.folder_id]
            }
            json_str = json.dumps(data, indent=2)
            media = MediaIoBaseUpload(io.BytesIO(json_str.encode('utf-8')), mimetype='application/json')
            
            file = self.service.files().create(
                body=file_metadata, 
                media_body=media, 
                fields='id'
            ).execute()
            
            logger.info(f"Drive Upload Success: {file.get('id')}")
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Drive Upload Failed: {e}")
            return False
EOF

# 2. REWRITE DSIE CORE (Integer Safety + Validation)
cat <<EOF > src/dsie_core.py
import logging
import google.generativeai as genai
from google.cloud import firestore
import os
import json
import datetime
from src.tools.drive import DriveClient

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")
# Explicit DB connection
db = firestore.Client(database="veiled-vector-core-firestore")

class DSIECore:
    def __init__(self):
        self.api_key = os.getenv("GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY")
        if self.api_key:
            genai.configure(api_key=self.api_key)
            # NUCLEAR SAFETY: Using Integers to bypass library enum mapping errors
            # 7=Harassment, 8=Hate, 9=Sexual, 10=Dangerous
            # 4=BLOCK_NONE
            safety = [
                {"category": 7, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 8, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 9, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 10, "threshold": 4}
            ]
            self.model = genai.GenerativeModel('gemini-2.0-flash-001', safety_settings=safety)
        self.drive = None

    def extract_json(self, text):
        import re
        match = re.search(r'\{.*\}', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match: return json.loads(match.group(0))
        match_list = re.search(r'\[.*\]', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match_list: return json.loads(match_list.group(0))
        raise ValueError("No JSON object found in LLM response")

    async def run_cycle(self, task: str):
        """ DISPATCHER """
        logger.info(f"DELEGATING MISSION: {task}")
        mission_id = f"mission_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d%H%M%S')}"
        doc_ref = db.collection("mission_queue").document(mission_id)
        doc_ref.set({
            "task": task,
            "status": "PENDING",
            "created_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP,
            "worker": "KAJI_DELL",
            "target_db": "veiled-vector-core-firestore"
        })
        return {"status": "Delegated to Dell", "mission_id": mission_id}

    async def process_pending_results(self):
        """ ANALYST """
        logger.info("Checking for completed missions...")
        docs = db.collection("mission_queue").where("status", "==", "COMPLETED").stream()
        
        processed_count = 0
        if not self.drive: self.drive = DriveClient()

        for doc in docs:
            data = doc.to_dict()
            if data.get("analysis_status") == "DONE": continue
            
            mission_id = doc.id
            logger.info(f"Processing Results for {mission_id}...")
            
            html_content = data.get("result_data", "")
            
            # DATA INTEGRITY AUDIT
            if len(html_content) < 500 or "Error" in data.get("result_title", ""):
                logger.warning(f"Data Integrity Failure for {mission_id}. Skipping.")
                doc.reference.update({"analysis_status": "REJECTED_BAD_DATA"})
                continue

            try:
                prompt = f"""
                Analyze this raw HTML data.
                Task: {data.get("task")}
                Extract the relevant odds/data into valid JSON.
                HTML Content (Truncated): {html_content[:50000]}
                """
                response = self.model.generate_content(prompt)
                parsed_data = self.extract_json(response.text)
                
                filename = f"{mission_id}_results.json"
                if self.drive.upload_json(filename, parsed_data):
                    doc.reference.update({
                        "analysis_status": "DONE",
                        "final_file": filename,
                        "analyzed_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP
                    })
                    processed_count += 1
                    logger.info(f"Mission {mission_id} Analyzed & Saved.")
                else:
                     logger.error(f"Drive Upload Failed for {mission_id}")
                
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Analysis Failed: {e}")
                doc.reference.update({"analysis_status": "FAILED", "error": str(e)})

        return {"status": "Batch Complete", "processed": processed_count}
EOF

Python
async def scrape_target(url: str):
    """
    Scrapes using Residential IP with Validation.
    """
    logger.info(f"Launching Browser for: {url}")
    async with async_playwright() as p:
        browser = await p.chromium.launch(headless=True)
        # Randomize Context
        context = await browser.new_context(
            user_agent="Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/120.0.0.0 Safari/537.36",
            viewport={"width": 1920, "height": 1080}
        )
        page = await context.new_page()
        
        try:
            await page.goto(url, timeout=60000, wait_until="domcontentloaded")
            await page.wait_for_timeout(5000) # Human pause
            
            content = await page.content()
            title = await page.title()
            
            # VALIDATION GATE
            if "Error" in title or "Captcha" in title or len(content) < 500:
                await browser.close()
                return {"status": "FAILED", "error": f"Soft Block Detected. Title: {title}"}
            
            # Clean HTML
            soup = BeautifulSoup(content, 'html.parser')
            for s in soup(["script", "style", "svg"]): s.extract()
            clean_text = soup.get_text(separator=' ', strip=True)[:80000]
            
            await browser.close()
            return {"status": "SUCCESS", "title": title, "data": clean_text}
            
        except Exception as e:
            await browser.close()
            return {"status": "FAILED", "error": str(e)}

async def process_mission(doc):
    mission_data = doc.to_dict()
    task = mission_data.get("task")
    
    # INTELLIGENT SEARCH ROUTING
    if "http" in task:
        target_url = task
    else:
        # USE GOOGLE, NOT DUCKDUCKGO
        # We use the 'q' parameter to jump straight to results
        query = task.replace(" ", "+")
        target_url = f"https://www.google.com/search?q={query}"
    
    logger.info(f"Executing: {target_url}")
    result = await scrape_target(target_url)
    
    if result["status"] == "SUCCESS":
        doc.reference.update({
            "status": "COMPLETED",
            "result_data": result["data"],
            "result_title": result["title"],
            "completed_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP
        })
        logger.info("Upload Complete.")
    else:
        logger.error(f"Failed: {result['error']}")
        doc.reference.update({"status": "FAILED", "error": result['error']})

Role Confirmed: VP of Engineering

Status: THE QUOTA TRAP.

I hear you. And I am looking at the error log you provided:

WARNING:googleapiclient.http:Encountered 403 Forbidden with reason "storageQuotaExceeded"

The Diagnosis: You are right—you gave the Service Account "Editor" permissions. However, in the Google Drive API, permissions do not grant Storage Quota.

The Trap: Service Accounts have 0 bytes of storage allocated to them by default.

The Failure: When the Service Account creates a file (even in your folder), Google treats the Service Account as the Owner of that file. It tries to deduct the file size from the Service Account's quota (which is zero). The upload fails.

Why it worked before: It didn't. We likely never successfully uploaded a file as the Service Account to a Personal Drive folder. This works seamlessly in "Google Workspace" (Shared Drives) where the Org owns the file, but fails in Personal Drive.

The Solution: The Infrastructure Pivot We are done fighting Google Drive's consumer-grade limitations. We are switching to Google Cloud Storage (GCS).

Why: GCS is the enterprise standard. It is native to the Service Account. It has no "quota" issues (it's pay-for-what-you-use). It is faster and reliable.

The Change: The Cloud Brain will upload the JSON results to a Storage Bucket instead of a Drive Folder.

PHASE 1: THE CLOUD FIX (v5.3 GCS Pivot)
This script rips out the Drive integration and replaces it with Google Cloud Storage.

Action: Run this in Cloud Shell.

Bash
#!/bin/bash

# ==========================================
# VEILED VECTOR INC. - v5.3 GCS PIVOT
# ==========================================
# Objective: Replace Drive with Cloud Storage (GCS)
# Target: veiled-vector-orchestrator

PROJECT_ID="veiled-vector-core"
SERVICE_NAME="veiled-vector-orchestrator"
REGION="us-central1"
# Create a unique bucket name
BUCKET_NAME="veiled-vector-data-${PROJECT_ID}"

echo "VECTOR_LOG: Initiating GCS Pivot..."

# 1. ENABLE STORAGE API
gcloud services enable storage.googleapis.com

# 2. CREATE BUCKET (If not exists)
if ! gcloud storage buckets list gs://${BUCKET_NAME} > /dev/null 2>&1; then
    echo "VECTOR_LOG: Creating Storage Bucket: ${BUCKET_NAME}"
    gcloud storage buckets create gs://${BUCKET_NAME} --location=$REGION
else
    echo "VECTOR_LOG: Bucket ${BUCKET_NAME} already exists."
fi

cd veiled-vector-cloud

# 3. UPDATE REQUIREMENTS (Add google-cloud-storage)

fastapi

google-cloud-storage
google-generativeai>=0.7.0

# 4. CREATE STORAGE TOOL (New)
cat <<EOF > src/tools/storage.py
import logging
from google.cloud import storage
import json

logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")

class StorageClient:
    def __init__(self):
        self.client = storage.Client()
        self.bucket_name = "${BUCKET_NAME}"
        self.bucket = self.client.bucket(self.bucket_name)

    def upload_json(self, filename: str, data: dict):
        try:
            blob = self.bucket.blob(f"results/{filename}")
            blob.upload_from_string(
                data=json.dumps(data, indent=2),
                content_type='application/json'
            )
            logger.info(f"GCS Upload Success: gs://{self.bucket_name}/results/{filename}")
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"GCS Upload Failed: {e}")
            return False
EOF

import logging
import google.generativeai as genai
from google.cloud import firestore
import os
import json

from src.tools.storage import StorageClient

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")

class DSIECore:
    def __init__(self):
        self.api_key = os.getenv("GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY")
        if self.api_key:
            genai.configure(api_key=self.api_key)
            # Integer-based safety settings (Nuclear option)
            safety = [
                {"category": 7, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 8, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 9, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 10, "threshold": 4}
            ]
            self.model = genai.GenerativeModel('gemini-2.0-flash-001', safety_settings=safety)
        self.storage = None

    def extract_json(self, text):
        import re
        match = re.search(r'\{.*\}', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match: return json.loads(match.group(0))
        match_list = re.search(r'\[.*\]', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match_list: return json.loads(match_list.group(0))
        raise ValueError("No JSON object found in LLM response")

    async def run_cycle(self, task: str):
        """ DISPATCHER """
        logger.info(f"DELEGATING MISSION: {task}")
        mission_id = f"mission_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d%H%M%S')}"
        doc_ref = db.collection("mission_queue").document(mission_id)
        doc_ref.set({
            "task": task,
            "status": "PENDING",
            "created_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP,
            "worker": "KAJI_DELL",
            "target_db": "veiled-vector-core-firestore"
        })
        return {"status": "Delegated to Dell", "mission_id": mission_id}

    async def process_pending_results(self):
        """ ANALYST """
        logger.info("Checking for completed missions...")
        docs = db.collection("mission_queue").where("status", "==", "COMPLETED").stream()
        
        processed_count = 0
        if not self.storage: self.storage = StorageClient()

        for doc in docs:
            data = doc.to_dict()
            if data.get("analysis_status") == "DONE": continue
            
            mission_id = doc.id
            logger.info(f"Processing Results for {mission_id}...")
            
            html_content = data.get("result_data", "")
            
            # DATA INTEGRITY: If HTML is tiny or error-filled, reject it.
            if len(html_content) < 500 or "Error" in data.get("result_title", ""):
                logger.warning(f"Data Integrity Failure for {mission_id}. Skipping.")
                doc.reference.update({"analysis_status": "REJECTED_BAD_DATA"})
                continue

            try:
                prompt = f"""
                Analyze this raw HTML data.
                Task: {data.get("task")}
                Extract the relevant odds/data into valid JSON.
                HTML Content (Truncated): {html_content[:50000]}
                """
                response = self.model.generate_content(prompt)
                parsed_data = self.extract_json(response.text)
                
                filename = f"{mission_id}_results.json"
                if self.storage.upload_json(filename, parsed_data):
                    doc.reference.update({
                        "analysis_status": "DONE",
                        "final_file": f"gs://veiled-vector-data-{PROJECT_ID}/results/{filename}",
                        "analyzed_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP
                    })
                    processed_count += 1
                    logger.info(f"Mission {mission_id} Analyzed & Saved to GCS.")
                else:
                     logger.error(f"Storage Upload Failed for {mission_id}")
                
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Analysis Failed: {e}")
                doc.reference.update({"analysis_status": "FAILED", "error": str(e)})

        return {"status": "Batch Complete", "processed": processed_count}
EOF

#!/bin/bash

# ==========================================
# VEILED VECTOR INC. - v5.3 GCS PIVOT
# ==========================================
# Objective: Replace Drive with Cloud Storage (GCS) to bypass quota errors
# Target: veiled-vector-orchestrator

PROJECT_ID="veiled-vector-core"
SERVICE_NAME="veiled-vector-orchestrator"
REGION="us-central1"
# Create a unique bucket name
BUCKET_NAME="veiled-vector-data-${PROJECT_ID}"

echo "VECTOR_LOG: Initiating GCS Pivot..."

# 1. ENABLE STORAGE API
gcloud services enable storage.googleapis.com

# 2. CREATE BUCKET (If not exists)
if ! gcloud storage buckets list gs://${BUCKET_NAME} > /dev/null 2>&1; then
    echo "VECTOR_LOG: Creating Storage Bucket: ${BUCKET_NAME}"
    gcloud storage buckets create gs://${BUCKET_NAME} --location=$REGION
else
    echo "VECTOR_LOG: Bucket ${BUCKET_NAME} already exists."
fi

cd veiled-vector-cloud

# 4. CREATE STORAGE TOOL (New)
cat <<EOF > src/tools/storage.py
import logging
from google.cloud import storage
import json

logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")

class StorageClient:
    def __init__(self):
        self.client = storage.Client()
        self.bucket_name = "${BUCKET_NAME}"
        self.bucket = self.client.bucket(self.bucket_name)

    def upload_json(self, filename: str, data: dict):
        try:
            blob = self.bucket.blob(f"results/{filename}")
            blob.upload_from_string(
                data=json.dumps(data, indent=2),
                content_type='application/json'
            )
            logger.info(f"GCS Upload Success: gs://{self.bucket_name}/results/{filename}")
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"GCS Upload Failed: {e}")
            return False
EOF

import logging
import google.generativeai as genai
from google.cloud import firestore
import os
import json
import datetime
from src.tools.storage import StorageClient

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")
db = firestore.Client(database="veiled-vector-core-firestore")

class DSIECore:
    def __init__(self):
        self.api_key = os.getenv("GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY")
        if self.api_key:
            genai.configure(api_key=self.api_key)
            # Integer Safety Settings (Block None)
            safety = [
                {"category": 7, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 8, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 9, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 10, "threshold": 4}
            ]
            self.model = genai.GenerativeModel('gemini-2.0-flash-001', safety_settings=safety)
        self.storage = None

    def extract_json(self, text):
        import re
        match = re.search(r'\{.*\}', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match: return json.loads(match.group(0))
        match_list = re.search(r'\[.*\]', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match_list: return json.loads(match_list.group(0))
        raise ValueError("No JSON object found in LLM response")

    async def run_cycle(self, task: str):
        """ DISPATCHER """
        logger.info(f"DELEGATING MISSION: {task}")
        mission_id = f"mission_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d%H%M%S')}"
        doc_ref = db.collection("mission_queue").document(mission_id)
        doc_ref.set({
            "task": task,
            "status": "PENDING",
            "created_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP,
            "worker": "KAJI_DELL",
            "target_db": "veiled-vector-core-firestore"
        })
        return {"status": "Delegated to Dell", "mission_id": mission_id}

    async def process_pending_results(self):
        """ ANALYST """
        logger.info("Checking for completed missions...")
        docs = db.collection("mission_queue").where("status", "==", "COMPLETED").stream()
        
        processed_count = 0
        if not self.storage: self.storage = StorageClient()

        for doc in docs:
            data = doc.to_dict()
            if data.get("analysis_status") == "DONE": continue
            
            mission_id = doc.id
            logger.info(f"Processing Results for {mission_id}...")
            
            html_content = data.get("result_data", "")
            
            # DATA INTEGRITY: Check for CAPTCHA/Blocks
            if "unusual traffic" in html_content or "CAPTCHA" in html_content or len(html_content) < 1000:
                logger.warning(f"Data Integrity Failure (CAPTCHA/Block) for {mission_id}. Rejecting.")
                doc.reference.update({"analysis_status": "REJECTED_BAD_DATA"})
                continue

            try:
                prompt = f"""
                Analyze this raw HTML data.
                Task: {data.get("task")}
                Extract the relevant odds/data into valid JSON.
                HTML Content (Truncated): {html_content[:60000]}
                """
                response = self.model.generate_content(prompt)
                parsed_data = self.extract_json(response.text)
                
                filename = f"{mission_id}_results.json"
                if self.storage.upload_json(filename, parsed_data):
                    doc.reference.update({
                        "analysis_status": "DONE",
                        "final_file": f"gs://veiled-vector-data-${PROJECT_ID}/results/{filename}",
                        "analyzed_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP
                    })
                    processed_count += 1
                    logger.info(f"Mission {mission_id} Analyzed & Saved to GCS.")
                else:
                     logger.error(f"Storage Upload Failed for {mission_id}")
                
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Analysis Failed: {e}")
                doc.reference.update({"analysis_status": "FAILED", "error": str(e)})

        return {"status": "Batch Complete", "processed": processed_count}
EOF

# nano worker.py -> Delete all -> Paste this
import os
import time
import json
import logging
import random
from google.cloud import firestore
from playwright.async_api import async_playwright
from fake_useragent import UserAgent
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
import asyncio

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - [KAJI-WORKER] - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
logger = logging.getLogger("KajiWorker")
os.environ["GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS"] = "credentials.json"
db = firestore.Client(database="veiled-vector-core-firestore")
ua = UserAgent()

async def scrape_target(url: str):
    logger.info(f"Navigating Direct to: {url}")
    async with async_playwright() as p:
        browser = await p.chromium.launch(headless=True)
        # Enhanced Stealth Context
        context = await browser.new_context(
            user_agent=ua.random,
            viewport={"width": 1920, "height": 1080},
            device_scale_factor=1,
        )
        # Evasion Scripts
        await context.add_init_script("Object.defineProperty(navigator, 'webdriver', {get: () => undefined})")
        
        page = await context.new_page()
        try:
            # Increased timeout for heavy sites
            await page.goto(url, timeout=90000, wait_until="domcontentloaded")
            await page.wait_for_timeout(random.randint(5000, 8000)) 
            
            content = await page.content()
            title = await page.title()
            
            # PRE-FLIGHT VALIDATION
            if "unusual traffic" in content or "Captcha" in title:
                await browser.close()
                return {"status": "FAILED", "error": "Detected Block/Captcha"}
            
            # Clean HTML
            soup = BeautifulSoup(content, 'html.parser')
            for s in soup(["script", "style", "svg", "img", "video"]): s.extract()
            clean_text = soup.get_text(separator=' ', strip=True)[:80000]
            
            await browser.close()
            return {"status": "SUCCESS", "title": title, "data": clean_text}
        except Exception as e:
            await browser.close()
            return {"status": "FAILED", "error": str(e)}

async def process_mission(doc):
    mission_data = doc.to_dict()
    task = mission_data.get("task")
    
    # INTELLIGENT ROUTING: SKIP SEARCH ENGINE
    if "http" in task:
        target_url = task
    else:
        # If asking for odds, go to OddsPortal directly
        if "odds" in task.lower():
            target_url = "https://www.oddsportal.com/american-football/usa/nfl/"
        else:
            target_url = f"https://www.google.com/search?q={task.replace(' ', '+')}"
    
    logger.info(f"Executing Mission: {target_url}")
    result = await scrape_target(target_url)
    
    if result["status"] == "SUCCESS":
        doc.reference.update({
            "status": "COMPLETED",
            "result_data": result["data"],
            "result_title": result["title"],
            "completed_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP
        })
        logger.info("Mission Success. Uploaded to Firestore.")
    else:
        logger.error(f"Mission Failed: {result['error']}")
        doc.reference.update({"status": "FAILED", "error": result['error']})

async def main_loop():
    logger.info("KAJI DIRECT-WORKER ONLINE. Waiting...")
    while True:
        docs = db.collection("mission_queue").where("status", "==", "PENDING").limit(1).stream()
        found = False
        for doc in docs:
            found = True
            await process_mission(doc)
        if not found: time.sleep(5)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    asyncio.run(main_loop())

import logging
from google.cloud import storage
import json

logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")

class StorageClient:
    def __init__(self):
        self.client = storage.Client()
        self.bucket_name = "${BUCKET_NAME}"
        self.bucket = self.client.bucket(self.bucket_name)

    def upload_json(self, filename: str, data: dict):
        try:
            blob = self.bucket.blob(f"results/{filename}")
            blob.upload_from_string(
                data=json.dumps(data, indent=2),
                content_type='application/json'
            )
            logger.info(f"GCS Upload Success: gs://{self.bucket_name}/results/{filename}")
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"GCS Upload Failed: {e}")
            return False
EOF

# 5. REWRITE DSIE CORE (With Data Integrity Checks)
cat <<EOF > src/dsie_core.py
import logging
import google.generativeai as genai
from google.cloud import firestore
import os
import json
import datetime
from src.tools.storage import StorageClient

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")
# Explicit DB connection to your custom ID
db = firestore.Client(database="veiled-vector-core-firestore")

class DSIECore:
    def __init__(self):
        self.api_key = os.getenv("GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY")
        if self.api_key:
            genai.configure(api_key=self.api_key)
            # NUCLEAR SAFETY: Integers to bypass library enum mapping errors
            # 7=Harassment, 8=Hate, 9=Sexual, 10=Dangerous
            # 4=BLOCK_NONE
            safety = [
                {"category": 7, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 8, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 9, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 10, "threshold": 4}
            ]
            # Using verified stable model 2.0
            self.model = genai.GenerativeModel('gemini-2.0-flash-001', safety_settings=safety)
        self.storage = None

    def extract_json(self, text):
        import re
        match = re.search(r'\{.*\}', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match: return json.loads(match.group(0))
        match_list = re.search(r'\[.*\]', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match_list: return json.loads(match_list.group(0))
        raise ValueError("No JSON object found in LLM response")

    async def run_cycle(self, task: str):
        """ DISPATCHER """
        logger.info(f"DELEGATING MISSION: {task}")
        mission_id = f"mission_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d%H%M%S')}"
        doc_ref = db.collection("mission_queue").document(mission_id)
        doc_ref.set({
            "task": task,
            "status": "PENDING",
            "created_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP,
            "worker": "KAJI_DELL",
            "target_db": "veiled-vector-core-firestore"
        })
        return {"status": "Delegated to Dell", "mission_id": mission_id}

    async def process_pending_results(self):
        """ ANALYST """
        logger.info("Checking for completed missions...")
        docs = db.collection("mission_queue").where("status", "==", "COMPLETED").stream()
        
        processed_count = 0
        if not self.storage: self.storage = StorageClient()

        for doc in docs:
            data = doc.to_dict()
            if data.get("analysis_status") == "DONE": continue
            
            mission_id = doc.id
            logger.info(f"Processing Results for {mission_id}...")
            
            html_content = data.get("result_data", "")
            
            # DATA INTEGRITY: Check for CAPTCHA/Blocks/Empty
            if "unusual traffic" in html_content or "CAPTCHA" in html_content or len(html_content) < 1000:
                logger.warning(f"Data Integrity Failure (CAPTCHA/Block) for {mission_id}. Rejecting.")
                doc.reference.update({"analysis_status": "REJECTED_BAD_DATA"})
                continue

            try:
                prompt = f"""
                Analyze this raw HTML data.
                Task: {data.get("task")}
                Extract the relevant odds/data into valid JSON.
                HTML Content (Truncated): {html_content[:60000]}
                """
                response = self.model.generate_content(prompt)
                parsed_data = self.extract_json(response.text)
                
                filename = f"{mission_id}_results.json"
                if self.storage.upload_json(filename, parsed_data):
                    doc.reference.update({
                        "analysis_status": "DONE",
                        "final_file": f"gs://veiled-vector-data-{PROJECT_ID}/results/{filename}",
                        "analyzed_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP
                    })
                    processed_count += 1
                    logger.info(f"Mission {mission_id} Analyzed & Saved to GCS.")
                else:
                     logger.error(f"Storage Upload Failed for {mission_id}")
                
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Analysis Failed: {e}")
                doc.reference.update({"analysis_status": "FAILED", "error": str(e)})

        return {"status": "Batch Complete", "processed": processed_count}
EOF

Technically Scrapable" Aggregators

These sites are commercial aggregators. They do not explicitly allow scraping, but they are widely known in the community to be lenient if you scrape slowly (low volume) or use tools like Selenium.

6. OddsPortal



URL: https://www.oddsportal.com/

Scraping Difficulty: Medium (Requires Selenium/Puppeteer)

Why: It is the most popular target for scrapers because it aggregates odds from 80+ bookies. It uses dynamic JavaScript, so you cannot use simple requests or BeautifulSoup; you must use a browser automation tool.

Tip: Look for "OddsPortal Scraper" repositories on GitHub; many exist because the community heavily uses this site.

7. BetExplorer



URL: https://www.betexplorer.com/

Scraping Difficulty: Low/Medium

Why: A sister site to OddsPortal with a slightly simpler layout. It is often preferred for historical results and odds because the URL structure is very predictable.

8. VegasInsider



URL: https://www.vegasinsider.com/odds/

Scraping Difficulty: Medium

Why: The go-to source for "Public Consensus" and Las Vegas odds. They have updated their site to be more dynamic, but the tables are still accessible via standard scraping tools. Essential for US sports (NFL, NBA, MLB).

9. OddsMath



URL: https://oddsmath.com/

Scraping Difficulty: Medium

Why: Excellent for tracking "dropping odds" and line movements. The interface is data-heavy, which actually makes it easier to parse once you locate the correct JSON endpoints in your browser's "Network" tab.

10. Flashscore



URL: https://www.flashscore.com/

Scraping Difficulty: High (Strict Anti-Bot)

Why include it? It is the most comprehensive data source globally. While they have strict anti-bot protections, low-volume scraping is possible if you use undetected-chromedriver or similar stealth tools.

Warning: They are more likely to block your IP than others on this list, so use a proxy if possible.

Technical Tips for Low Volume Scraping

To ensure you stay "low volume" and don't get blocked:



Set a User-Agent: Never use the default Python/scraper User-Agent. Set it to a standard browser:'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36'

Randomize Delays: Sleep for random.uniform(3, 7) seconds between requests.

Cache Requests: If you are testing your code, save the HTML to a local file first so you don't hit their server every time you fix a bug in your parser.

import os
import time
import json
import logging
import random
from google.cloud import firestore
from playwright.async_api import async_playwright
from fake_useragent import UserAgent
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
import asyncio

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - [KAJI-WORKER] - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
logger = logging.getLogger("KajiWorker")
os.environ["GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS"] = "credentials.json"
# Ensure this matches your specific DB
db = firestore.Client(database="veiled-vector-core-firestore")
ua = UserAgent()

# REDUNDANCY LIST
TARGETS = [
    "https://www.oddsportal.com/american-football/usa/nfl/",
    "https://www.betexplorer.com/football/usa/nfl/",
    "https://www.vegasinsider.com/nfl/odds/las-vegas/"
]

async def scrape_url(url: str):
    logger.info(f"Attempting Target: {url}")
    async with async_playwright() as p:
        browser = await p.chromium.launch(headless=True)
        context = await browser.new_context(
            user_agent=ua.random,
            viewport={"width": 1920, "height": 1080},
            device_scale_factor=1,
        )
        await context.add_init_script("Object.defineProperty(navigator, 'webdriver', {get: () => undefined})")
        
        page = await context.new_page()
        try:
            # Increased timeout for stability
            await page.goto(url, timeout=60000, wait_until="domcontentloaded")
            await page.wait_for_timeout(random.randint(5000, 10000)) 
            
            content = await page.content()
            title = await page.title()
            
            # VALIDATION: Check for soft blocks
            if "unusual traffic" in content or "Captcha" in title or "403 Forbidden" in title:
                await browser.close()
                return {"status": "BLOCKED", "error": f"Soft Block on {url}"}
            
            # Clean HTML to save bandwidth
            soup = BeautifulSoup(content, 'html.parser')
            for s in soup(["script", "style", "svg", "img", "video", "iframe"]): s.extract()
            clean_text = soup.get_text(separator=' ', strip=True)[:90000]
            
            await browser.close()
            return {"status": "SUCCESS", "title": title, "data": clean_text}
        except Exception as e:
            await browser.close()
            return {"status": "ERROR", "error": str(e)}

async def process_mission(doc):
    mission_data = doc.to_dict()
    task = mission_data.get("task")
    
    # FAILOVER LOGIC
    final_result = None
    
    # If user provided a specific URL, prioritize it. Otherwise, cycle through targets.
    if "http" in task:
        target_list = [task]
    elif "odds" in task.lower() and "bills" in task.lower():
        target_list = TARGETS
    else:
        # Fallback to Google if it's not an odds request
        target_list = [f"https://www.google.com/search?q={task.replace(' ', '+')}"]

    for url in target_list:
        result = await scrape_url(url)
        if result["status"] == "SUCCESS":
            final_result = result
            logger.info(f"Success at {url}")
            break
        else:
            logger.warning(f"Failed at {url}: {result['error']}. Rolling to next target...")
            time.sleep(5) # Cool down between jumps

    if final_result:
        doc.reference.update({
            "status": "COMPLETED",
            "result_data": final_result["data"],
            "result_title": final_result["title"],
            "source_url": url,
            "completed_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP
        })
        logger.info("Mission Complete. Data Uploaded.")
    else:
        logger.error("All Targets Failed.")
        doc.reference.update({"status": "FAILED", "error": "All targets exhausted/blocked."})

async def main_loop():
    logger.info("KAJI MULTI-TARGET WORKER ONLINE.")
    while True:
        try:
            docs = db.collection("mission_queue").where("status", "==", "PENDING").limit(1).stream()
            found = False
            for doc in docs:
                found = True
                await process_mission(doc)
            if not found: time.sleep(5)
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Main Loop Error: {e}")
            time.sleep(10)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    asyncio.run(main_loop())

Python
import os
import time
import json
import logging
import random
from google.cloud import firestore
from playwright.async_api import async_playwright
from fake_useragent import UserAgent
import asyncio
import base64

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - [KAJI-WORKER] - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
logger = logging.getLogger("KajiWorker")
os.environ["GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS"] = "credentials.json"
db = firestore.Client(database="veiled-vector-core-firestore")
ua = UserAgent()

async def scrape_target(url: str):
    logger.info(f"Targeting: {url}")
    async with async_playwright() as p:
        browser = await p.chromium.launch(headless=True)
        context = await browser.new_context(
            user_agent=ua.random,
            viewport={"width": 1920, "height": 1080},
            device_scale_factor=1,
        )
        # Bypass some bot detections
        await context.add_init_script("Object.defineProperty(navigator, 'webdriver', {get: () => undefined})")
        
        page = await context.new_page()
        try:
            # Load the page
            await page.goto(url, timeout=60000, wait_until="domcontentloaded")
            
            # Wait for the ODDS to physically render
            # We wait for a generic class that usually holds match data to ensure hydration
            try:
                await page.wait_for_selector("div[class*='flex']", timeout=15000)
            except:
                logger.warning("Could not find specific match selectors, proceeding with full dump.")
            
            await page.wait_for_timeout(5000) # Extra buffer
            
            # 1. CAPTURE EVIDENCE (Screenshot)
            screenshot_bytes = await page.screenshot(full_page=False)
            screenshot_b64 = base64.b64encode(screenshot_bytes).decode('utf-8')
            
            # 2. CAPTURE RAW DATA (No Cleaning)
            content = await page.content()
            title = await page.title()
            
            await browser.close()
            
            # We return the FULL HTML. It's heavy, but it contains the hidden JSON state.
            return {
                "status": "SUCCESS", 
                "title": title, 
                "data": content, # RAW HTML
                "screenshot": screenshot_b64 
            }
        except Exception as e:
            await browser.close()
            return {"status": "FAILED", "error": str(e)}

async def process_mission(doc):
    mission_data = doc.to_dict()
    task = mission_data.get("task")
    
    # Direct Target
    target_url = "https://www.oddsportal.com/american-football/usa/nfl/"
    
    logger.info(f"Executing: {target_url}")
    result = await scrape_target(target_url)
    
    if result["status"] == "SUCCESS":
        # Verify we actually got data, not just a title
        if len(result["data"]) < 5000:
             logger.error("Page suspiciously small. Likely blocked.")
             doc.reference.update({"status": "FAILED", "error": "Soft Block (Empty Body)"})
             return

        doc.reference.update({
            "status": "COMPLETED",
            "result_data": result["data"], # Raw HTML
            "result_title": result["title"],
            "result_screenshot": result["screenshot"], # Visual Proof
            "completed_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP
        })
        logger.info("Mission Success. Raw Data Uploaded.")
    else:
        logger.error(f"Mission Failed: {result['error']}")
        doc.reference.update({"status": "FAILED", "error": result['error']})

async def main_loop():
    logger.info("KAJI RAW-WORKER ONLINE.")
    while True:
        try:
            docs = db.collection("mission_queue").where("status", "==", "PENDING").limit(1).stream()
            found = False
            for doc in docs:
                found = True
                await process_mission(doc)
            if not found: time.sleep(5)
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Loop Error: {e}")
            time.sleep(10)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    asyncio.run(main_loop())

Role Confirmed: VP of Engineering

The failure is logical, and it is my fault.

The Diagnosis:

"You definitely grabbed data": The scraping worked. The logs showed success.

"Status is FAILED": The write to Firestore failed.

"Project ID is empty": This is a symptom of a crashed write operation or a credential loading issue.

The Root Cause: The Firestore Physics Violation. I commanded the Dell to write Raw HTML (approx 500kb-2MB for a site like OddsPortal) PLUS a Base64 Screenshot (approx 2MB-5MB) directly into a single Firestore Document. Firestore has a hard limit of 1MB per document. The Worker tried to shove an elephant into a suitcase. The API rejected the payload, the Python script caught the exception, and marked the mission as FAILED (or crashed halfway through, leaving fields empty).

The Fix: "Heavy Lifting" Protocol (v5.4) We cannot put the raw data in Firestore.

The Dell must upload the HTML and Screenshot directly to Google Cloud Storage (GCS).

The Dell writes only the File Links (gs://...) to Firestore.

The Cloud Brain reads the files from GCS.

This bypasses the 1MB limit and fixes the "Project ID" issue by explicit declaration.

Python
import os
import time
import json
import logging
import random
from google.cloud import firestore
from google.cloud import storage
from playwright.async_api import async_playwright
from fake_useragent import UserAgent
import asyncio
import datetime

# LOGGING SETUP
logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - [KAJI-WORKER] - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
logger = logging.getLogger("KajiWorker")

# CONFIG
PROJECT_ID = "veiled-vector-core"
BUCKET_NAME = f"veiled-vector-data-{PROJECT_ID}"
CREDENTIALS_PATH = "credentials.json"

# FORCE ENV VARS
os.environ["GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS"] = CREDENTIALS_PATH
os.environ["GCLOUD_PROJECT"] = PROJECT_ID

# CLIENTS
# Explicit Project ID prevents "Empty Project ID" errors
db = firestore.Client(project=PROJECT_ID, database="veiled-vector-core-firestore")
storage_client = storage.Client(project=PROJECT_ID)
bucket = storage_client.bucket(BUCKET_NAME)
ua = UserAgent()

async def scrape_target(url: str):
    logger.info(f"Targeting: {url}")
    async with async_playwright() as p:
        browser = await p.chromium.launch(headless=True)
        context = await browser.new_context(
            user_agent=ua.random,
            viewport={"width": 1920, "height": 1080}
        )
        await context.add_init_script("Object.defineProperty(navigator, 'webdriver', {get: () => undefined})")
        
        page = await context.new_page()
        try:
            await page.goto(url, timeout=90000, wait_until="domcontentloaded")
            
            # Wait for odds/data table
            try:
                await page.wait_for_selector("div", timeout=10000)
            except: pass
            
            await page.wait_for_timeout(5000)
            
            # 1. CAPTURE SCREENSHOT (Binary)
            screenshot_bytes = await page.screenshot(full_page=True)
            
            # 2. CAPTURE HTML
            content = await page.content()
            title = await page.title()
            
            await browser.close()
            
            return {
                "status": "SUCCESS", 
                "title": title, 
                "html": content,
                "screenshot": screenshot_bytes
            }
        except Exception as e:
            await browser.close()
            return {"status": "FAILED", "error": str(e)}

def upload_to_gcs(mission_id, html_content, screenshot_bytes):
    """Uploads heavy assets to GCS and returns URIs."""
    try:
        # Upload HTML
        html_blob = bucket.blob(f"raw_data/{mission_id}.html")
        html_blob.upload_from_string(html_content, content_type="text/html")
        html_uri = f"gs://{BUCKET_NAME}/raw_data/{mission_id}.html"

        # Upload Screenshot
        shot_blob = bucket.blob(f"raw_data/{mission_id}.png")
        shot_blob.upload_from_string(screenshot_bytes, content_type="image/png")
        shot_uri = f"gs://{BUCKET_NAME}/raw_data/{mission_id}.png"
        
        return html_uri, shot_uri
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"GCS Upload Failed: {e}")
        return None, None

async def process_mission(doc):
    mission_id = doc.id
    mission_data = doc.to_dict()
    task = mission_data.get("task")
    
    # DIRECT ROUTING
    if "odds" in task.lower():
        target_url = "https://www.oddsportal.com/american-football/usa/nfl/"
    elif "http" in task:
        target_url = task
    else:
        target_url = f"https://www.google.com/search?q={task.replace(' ', '+')}"
    
    logger.info(f"Executing {mission_id}: {target_url}")
    result = await scrape_target(target_url)
    
    if result["status"] == "SUCCESS":
        # HEAVY LIFT: Upload to GCS
        html_uri, shot_uri = upload_to_gcs(mission_id, result["html"], result["screenshot"])
        
        if html_uri:
            doc.reference.update({
                "status": "COMPLETED",
                "result_title": result["title"],
                "gcs_html_uri": html_uri,       # Link to HTML
                "gcs_screenshot_uri": shot_uri, # Link to Screenshot
                "completed_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP
            })
            logger.info("Mission Success. Links Uploaded.")
        else:
            doc.reference.update({"status": "FAILED", "error": "GCS Upload Failed"})
    else:
        logger.error(f"Mission Failed: {result['error']}")
        doc.reference.update({"status": "FAILED", "error": result['error']})

async def main_loop():
    logger.info(f"KAJI HEAVY-LIFT WORKER ONLINE (Project: {PROJECT_ID})")
    while True:
        try:
            docs = db.collection("mission_queue").where("status", "==", "PENDING").limit(1).stream()
            found = False
            for doc in docs:
                found = True
                await process_mission(doc)
            if not found: time.sleep(5)
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Loop Error: {e}")
            time.sleep(10)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    asyncio.run(main_loop())

#!/bin/bash
# VEILED VECTOR INC. - v5.4 ANALYST UPGRADE

cat <<EOF > src/dsie_core.py
import logging
import google.generativeai as genai
from google.cloud import firestore
from google.cloud import storage
import os
import json
from src.tools.storage import StorageClient

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")
db = firestore.Client(database="veiled-vector-core-firestore")
gcs = storage.Client()

class DSIECore:
    def __init__(self):
        self.api_key = os.getenv("GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY")
        if self.api_key:
            genai.configure(api_key=self.api_key)
            safety = [
                {"category": 7, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 8, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 9, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 10, "threshold": 4}
            ]
            self.model = genai.GenerativeModel('gemini-2.0-flash-001', safety_settings=safety)
        self.storage = None

    def extract_json(self, text):
        import re
        match = re.search(r'\{.*\}', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match: return json.loads(match.group(0))
        match_list = re.search(r'\[.*\]', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match_list: return json.loads(match_list.group(0))
        raise ValueError("No JSON object found")

    async def run_cycle(self, task: str):
        # Dispatcher Logic... (Same as before)
        pass 

    async def process_pending_results(self):
        logger.info("Checking for completed missions...")
        docs = db.collection("mission_queue").where("status", "==", "COMPLETED").stream()
        processed_count = 0
        if not self.storage: self.storage = StorageClient()

        for doc in docs:
            data = doc.to_dict()
            if data.get("analysis_status") == "DONE": continue
            
            mission_id = doc.id
            # RETRIEVE FROM GCS
            html_uri = data.get("gcs_html_uri")
            if not html_uri:
                logger.warning(f"No HTML URI for {mission_id}")
                continue

            logger.info(f"Downloading HTML from {html_uri}...")
            try:
                # Parse URI
                blob_path = html_uri.replace(f"gs://{BUCKET_NAME}/", "")
                blob = gcs.bucket(BUCKET_NAME).blob(blob_path)
                html_content = blob.download_as_text()

                prompt = f"""
                Analyze this raw HTML.
                Task: {data.get("task")}
                Extract relevant odds/data into valid JSON.
                HTML Content (Truncated): {html_content[:80000]}
                """
                response = self.model.generate_content(prompt)
                parsed_data = self.extract_json(response.text)
                
                # SAVE RESULT
                filename = f"{mission_id}_results.json"
                self.storage.upload_json(filename, parsed_data)
                
                doc.reference.update({
                    "analysis_status": "DONE",
                    "final_file": f"gs://{BUCKET_NAME}/results/{filename}"
                })
                processed_count += 1
                logger.info(f"Success: {mission_id}")

            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Processing Failed: {e}")
                doc.reference.update({"analysis_status": "FAILED", "error": str(e)})

        return {"status": "Batch Complete", "processed": processed_count}
EOF

cat <<EOF > src/dsie_core.py
import logging
import google.generativeai as genai
from google.cloud import firestore
import os
import json
import datetime
from src.tools.storage import StorageClient

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")
db = firestore.Client(database="veiled-vector-core-firestore")

# HARDCODED CONFIGURATION
PROJECT_ID = "${PROJECT_ID}" 
BUCKET_NAME = "${BUCKET_NAME}"

class DSIECore:
    def __init__(self):
        self.api_key = os.getenv("GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY")
        if self.api_key:
            genai.configure(api_key=self.api_key)
            # Safety: Block None
            safety = [
                {"category": 7, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 8, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 9, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 10, "threshold": 4}
            ]
            self.model = genai.GenerativeModel('gemini-2.0-flash-001', safety_settings=safety)
        self.storage = None

    def extract_json(self, text):
        import re
        match = re.search(r'\{.*\}', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match: return json.loads(match.group(0))
        match_list = re.search(r'\[.*\]', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match_list: return json.loads(match_list.group(0))
        raise ValueError("No JSON object found in LLM response")

    async def run_cycle(self, task: str):
        """ DISPATCHER """
        logger.info(f"DELEGATING MISSION: {task}")
        mission_id = f"mission_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d%H%M%S')}"
        doc_ref = db.collection("mission_queue").document(mission_id)
        doc_ref.set({
            "task": task,
            "status": "PENDING",
            "created_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP,
            "worker": "KAJI_DELL",
            "target_db": "veiled-vector-core-firestore"
        })
        return {"status": "Delegated to Dell", "mission_id": mission_id}

    async def process_pending_results(self):
        """ ANALYST """
        logger.info("Checking for completed missions...")
        # Look for COMPLETED missions (Dell finished) OR FAILED missions (Retry analysis)
        # We specifically want to retry the one that just failed analysis
        docs = db.collection("mission_queue").where("status", "==", "COMPLETED").stream()
        
        processed_count = 0
        if not self.storage: self.storage = StorageClient()

        for doc in docs:
            data = doc.to_dict()
            # Skip if already analyzed successfully
            if data.get("analysis_status") == "DONE": continue
            
            mission_id = doc.id
            logger.info(f"Processing Results for {mission_id}...")
            
            # The Dell (v5.4) puts raw HTML in 'result_data' (if small) OR 'gcs_html_uri' (if large)
            # We need to handle both.
            
            html_content = data.get("result_data", "")
            
            # Basic Data Integrity Check
            if not html_content or len(html_content) < 100:
                 logger.warning(f"Empty Data for {mission_id}. Skipping.")
                 continue

            try:
                prompt = f"""
                Analyze this raw HTML data.
                Task: {data.get("task")}
                Extract the relevant odds/data into valid JSON.
                HTML Content (Truncated): {html_content[:60000]}
                """
                response = self.model.generate_content(prompt)
                parsed_data = self.extract_json(response.text)
                
                filename = f"{mission_id}_results.json"
                if self.storage.upload_json(filename, parsed_data):
                    doc.reference.update({
                        "analysis_status": "DONE",
                        # FIX: Use the global variable defined at top
                        "final_file": f"gs://{BUCKET_NAME}/results/{filename}",
                        "analyzed_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP
                    })
                    processed_count += 1
                    logger.info(f"Mission {mission_id} Analyzed & Saved to GCS.")
                else:
                     logger.error(f"Storage Upload Failed for {mission_id}")
                
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Analysis Failed: {e}")
                doc.reference.update({"analysis_status": "FAILED", "error": str(e)})

        return {"status": "Batch Complete", "processed": processed_count}
EOF

import logging
import google.generativeai as genai
from google.cloud import firestore
import os
import json
import datetime
from src.tools.storage import StorageClient

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")
db = firestore.Client(database="veiled-vector-core-firestore")

# HARDCODED CONFIGURATION (Injecting Bash vars into Python string)
PROJECT_ID = "${PROJECT_ID}" 
BUCKET_NAME = "${BUCKET_NAME}"

class DSIECore:
    def __init__(self):
        self.api_key = os.getenv("GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY")
        if self.api_key:
            genai.configure(api_key=self.api_key)
            # Safety: Block None
            safety = [
                {"category": 7, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 8, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 9, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 10, "threshold": 4}
            ]
            self.model = genai.GenerativeModel('gemini-2.0-flash-001', safety_settings=safety)
        self.storage = None

    def extract_json(self, text):
        import re
        match = re.search(r'\{.*\}', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match: return json.loads(match.group(0))
        match_list = re.search(r'\[.*\]', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match_list: return json.loads(match_list.group(0))
        raise ValueError("No JSON object found in LLM response")

    async def run_cycle(self, task: str):
        """ DISPATCHER """
        logger.info(f"DELEGATING MISSION: {task}")
        mission_id = f"mission_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d%H%M%S')}"
        doc_ref = db.collection("mission_queue").document(mission_id)
        doc_ref.set({
            "task": task,
            "status": "PENDING",
            "created_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP,
            "worker": "KAJI_DELL",
            "target_db": "veiled-vector-core-firestore"
        })
        return {"status": "Delegated to Dell", "mission_id": mission_id}

    async def process_pending_results(self):
        """ ANALYST """
        logger.info("Checking for completed missions...")
        # Process COMPLETED (Dell done) OR FAILED (Brain crashed previously)
        # We check for anything that has data but isn't marked DONE
        docs = db.collection("mission_queue").where("status", "==", "COMPLETED").stream()
        
        processed_count = 0
        if not self.storage: self.storage = StorageClient()

        for doc in docs:
            data = doc.to_dict()
            if data.get("analysis_status") == "DONE": continue
            
            mission_id = doc.id
            logger.info(f"Processing Results for {mission_id}...")
            
            html_content = data.get("result_data", "")
            
            if not html_content or len(html_content) < 100:
                 logger.warning(f"Empty Data for {mission_id}. Skipping.")
                 continue

            try:
                prompt = f"""
                Analyze this raw HTML data.
                Task: {data.get("task")}
                Extract the relevant odds/data into valid JSON.
                HTML Content (Truncated): {html_content[:60000]}
                """
                response = self.model.generate_content(prompt)
                parsed_data = self.extract_json(response.text)
                
                filename = f"{mission_id}_results.json"
                if self.storage.upload_json(filename, parsed_data):
                    # HERE IS THE FIX: Use the Python variable BUCKET_NAME defined above
                    final_path = f"gs://{BUCKET_NAME}/results/{filename}"
                    
                    doc.reference.update({
                        "analysis_status": "DONE",
                        "final_file": final_path,
                        "analyzed_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP
                    })
                    processed_count += 1
                    logger.info(f"Mission {mission_id} Analyzed & Saved to GCS.")
                else:
                     logger.error(f"Storage Upload Failed for {mission_id}")
                
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Analysis Failed: {e}")
                doc.reference.update({"analysis_status": "FAILED", "error": str(e)})

        return {"status": "Batch Complete", "processed": processed_count}

import os
import time

import random

import asyncio
import datetime

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - [KAJI-WORKER] - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
logger = logging.getLogger("KajiWorker")

# CONFIG
PROJECT_ID = "veiled-vector-core"
BUCKET_NAME = f"veiled-vector-data-{PROJECT_ID}"
CREDENTIALS_PATH = "credentials.json"

os.environ["GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS"] = CREDENTIALS_PATH
os.environ["GCLOUD_PROJECT"] = PROJECT_ID

# CLIENTS
db = firestore.Client(project=PROJECT_ID, database="veiled-vector-core-firestore")
storage_client = storage.Client(project=PROJECT_ID)
bucket = storage_client.bucket(BUCKET_NAME)
ua = UserAgent()

async def scrape_target(url: str, search_term: str = None):
    logger.info(f"Targeting: {url}")
    async with async_playwright() as p:
        browser = await p.chromium.launch(headless=True)
        context = await browser.new_context(
            user_agent=ua.random,
            viewport={"width": 1920, "height": 1080}
        )
        await context.add_init_script("Object.defineProperty(navigator, 'webdriver', {get: () => undefined})")
        
        page = await context.new_page()
        try:
            # 1. Go to the League Page
            await page.goto(url, timeout=90000, wait_until="domcontentloaded")
            await page.wait_for_timeout(5000)

            # 2. "HUNTER" LOGIC: Find and Click the specific game
            if search_term:
                logger.info(f"Hunting for match involving: {search_term}")
                try:
                    # Look for a link containing the team name
                    # We click the *first* occurrence that looks like a match link
                    # This navigates us from the 'Menu' to the 'Meal'
                    await page.click(f"a:has-text('{search_term}')", timeout=10000)
                    logger.info("Link found and clicked. Navigating to Match Page...")
                    
                    # Wait for the new page (Match Page) to load
                    await page.wait_for_load_state("domcontentloaded")
                    await page.wait_for_timeout(5000) # Wait for dynamic odds table
                except Exception as click_err:
                    logger.warning(f"Could not click specific team link: {click_err}. Scraping current page as fallback.")

            # 3. CAPTURE
            screenshot_bytes = await page.screenshot(full_page=True)
            content = await page.content()
            title = await page.title()
            
            await browser.close()
            
            return {
                "status": "SUCCESS", 
                "title": title, 
                "html": content,
                "screenshot": screenshot_bytes
            }
        except Exception as e:
            await browser.close()
            return {"status": "FAILED", "error": str(e)}

def upload_to_gcs(mission_id, html_content, screenshot_bytes):
    try:
        html_blob = bucket.blob(f"raw_data/{mission_id}.html")
        html_blob.upload_from_string(html_content, content_type="text/html")
        html_uri = f"gs://{BUCKET_NAME}/raw_data/{mission_id}.html"

        shot_blob = bucket.blob(f"raw_data/{mission_id}.png")
        shot_blob.upload_from_string(screenshot_bytes, content_type="image/png")
        shot_uri = f"gs://{BUCKET_NAME}/raw_data/{mission_id}.png"
        
        return html_uri, shot_uri
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"GCS Upload Failed: {e}")
        return None, None

async def process_mission(doc):
    mission_id = doc.id
    mission_data = doc.to_dict()
    task = mission_data.get("task")
    
    # Extract Team Name for "Hunter" Logic
    search_term = None
    if "Bills" in task: search_term = "Bills"
    elif "Buffalo" in task: search_term = "Buffalo"
    
    # DIRECT ROUTING
    if "http" in task:
        target_url = task
        search_term = None # Don't click if direct URL provided
    elif "odds" in task.lower():
        target_url = "https://www.oddsportal.com/american-football/usa/nfl/"
    else:
        target_url = f"https://www.google.com/search?q={task.replace(' ', '+')}"
    
    logger.info(f"Executing {mission_id}: {target_url}")
    result = await scrape_target(target_url, search_term)
    
    if result["status"] == "SUCCESS":
        html_uri, shot_uri = upload_to_gcs(mission_id, result["html"], result["screenshot"])
        if html_uri:
            doc.reference.update({
                "status": "COMPLETED",
                "result_title": result["title"],
                "gcs_html_uri": html_uri,
                "gcs_screenshot_uri": shot_uri,
                "completed_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP
            })
            logger.info("Mission Success. Links Uploaded.")
        else:
            doc.reference.update({"status": "FAILED", "error": "GCS Upload Failed"})
    else:
        logger.error(f"Mission Failed: {result['error']}")
        doc.reference.update({"status": "FAILED", "error": result['error']})

async def main_loop():
    logger.info(f"KAJI HUNTER-WORKER ONLINE (Project: {PROJECT_ID})")
    while True:
        try:
            docs = db.collection("mission_queue").where("status", "==", "PENDING").limit(1).stream()
            found = False
            for doc in docs:
                found = True
                await process_mission(doc)
            if not found: time.sleep(5)
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Loop Error: {e}")
            time.sleep(10)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    asyncio.run(main_loop())
