# REWRITE DSIE CORE (Recursive Dispatcher)
cat <<EOF > src/dsie_core.py
import logging
import google.generativeai as genai
from google.cloud import firestore
import os
import json
import datetime
import re
from src.tools.storage import StorageClient

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")
db = firestore.Client(database="veiled-vector-core-firestore")

PROJECT_ID = "${PROJECT_ID}" 
BUCKET_NAME = "${BUCKET_NAME}"

class DSIECore:
    def __init__(self):
        self.api_key = os.getenv("GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY")
        if self.api_key:
            genai.configure(api_key=self.api_key)
            # Safety: Block None
            safety = [
                {"category": 7, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 8, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 9, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 10, "threshold": 4}
            ]
            self.model = genai.GenerativeModel('gemini-2.0-flash-001', safety_settings=safety)
        self.storage = None

    def extract_json(self, text):
        match = re.search(r'\{.*\}', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match: return json.loads(match.group(0))
        match_list = re.search(r'\[.*\]', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match_list: return json.loads(match_list.group(0))
        # Fallback: Try to find key-value pairs if JSON is broken
        return {"raw_text": text[:1000], "error": "JSON Parsing Failed"}

    async def run_cycle(self, task: str):
        """ DISPATCHER """
        logger.info(f"DELEGATING MISSION: {task}")
        mission_id = f"mission_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d%H%M%S')}"
        doc_ref = db.collection("mission_queue").document(mission_id)
        doc_ref.set({
            "task": task,
            "status": "PENDING",
            "created_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP,
            "worker": "KAJI_DELL",
            "target_db": "veiled-vector-core-firestore"
        })
        return {"status": "Delegated to Dell", "mission_id": mission_id}

    async def process_pending_results(self):
        """ ANALYST """
        logger.info("Checking for completed missions...")
        docs = db.collection("mission_queue").where("status", "==", "COMPLETED").stream()
        
        processed_count = 0
        if not self.storage: self.storage = StorageClient()

        for doc in docs:
            data = doc.to_dict()
            if data.get("analysis_status") == "DONE": continue
            
            mission_id = doc.id
            logger.info(f"Processing Results for {mission_id}...")
            
            html_content = data.get("result_data", "")
            if not html_content or len(html_content) < 100:
                 logger.warning(f"Empty Data for {mission_id}. Skipping.")
                 continue

            try:
                # 1. ANALYZE
                prompt = f"""
                Analyze this raw HTML data.
                Original Task: {data.get("task")}
                
                OBJECTIVE: Extract betting odds for the Buffalo Bills.
                
                IF you see a specific match URL for the Bills but NO odds values (moneyline, spread), 
                OUTPUT JSON: {{ "action": "RECURSE", "target_url": "THE_URL_YOU_FOUND" }}
                
                IF you see the actual odds numbers, OUTPUT JSON with the stats.
                
                HTML Content (Truncated): {html_content[:60000]}
                """
                response = self.model.generate_content(prompt)
                parsed_data = self.extract_json(response.text)
                
                # 2. RECURSIVE LOGIC
                if parsed_data.get("action") == "RECURSE":
                    target_url = parsed_data.get("target_url")
                    logger.info(f"RECURSION TRIGGERED: Targeting {target_url}")
                    
                    # Create a new high-priority mission for the specific URL
                    new_mission_id = f"mission_sub_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%H%M%S')}"
                    db.collection("mission_queue").document(new_mission_id).set({
                        "task": target_url, # Worker handles URLs directly
                        "status": "PENDING",
                        "created_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP,
                        "worker": "KAJI_DELL",
                        "target_db": "veiled-vector-core-firestore",
                        "parent_mission": mission_id
                    })
                    doc.reference.update({"analysis_status": "RECURSING"})
                    
                else:
                    # 3. SAVE FINAL RESULT
                    filename = f"{mission_id}_results.json"
                    if self.storage.upload_json(filename, parsed_data):
                        final_path = f"gs://${BUCKET_NAME}/results/{filename}"
                        doc.reference.update({
                            "analysis_status": "DONE",
                            "final_file": final_path,
                            "analyzed_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP
                        })
                        logger.info(f"Mission {mission_id} Analyzed & Saved.")

                processed_count += 1
                
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Analysis Failed: {e}")
                doc.reference.update({"analysis_status": "FAILED", "error": str(e)})

        return {"status": "Batch Complete", "processed": processed_count}
EOF

Status: ANSWERING THE "WHY" & PROPOSING THE "FINAL PIVOT."

You asked the million-dollar question. Why can Gemini (the product) effortlessly browse these sites in "Deep Research" mode, but the Python script Gemini (the coder) writes for you fails miserably?

The answer is Identity & Infrastructure.

1. The "God Mode" Difference (Gemini Deep Research)
When you use Gemini Advanced/Deep Research, you are not browsing the web as a "User." You are browsing as Google.

Whitelisting: Most sites (OddsPortal, ESPN, DraftKings) explicitly whitelist Google's crawler IPs because they want to be indexed for SEO. They let Google in the front door while locking the side door you are trying to pick.

Proprietary Tech: Google's internal browsing infrastructure (which powers Deep Research) is not using standard Selenium/Playwright. It uses a highly advanced, proprietary headless browser with a TLS fingerprint that is virtually indistinguishable from a billion legitimate Chrome users.

Scale: Google hits them from thousands of IPs. If one gets blocked, it rotates instantly.

2. The "Junior Dev" Script (What We Built)
When Gemini writes a script for you, it is forced to use Open Source Tools (Playwright, Selenium, Python Requests).

The Fingerprint: These tools have "tells." Even with fake-useragent, the TLS handshake (JA3 fingerprint) often screams "I AM A PYTHON SCRIPT."

The Hostility: Sportsbooks spend millions on Cloudflare/Datadome specifically to block these specific tools. They don't block Google; they block scripts.

The Dell: Your Dell is a single residential IP. It is "clean," but it is static. If Playwright leaks a single "bot signal" (like executing JS too fast), the site flags your specific IP.

The fact that we got the schedule (JSON) proves we are not IP blocked.

cat <<EOF > src/dsie_core.py
import logging
import google.generativeai as genai
from google.cloud import firestore
from google.cloud import storage
import os
import json
import datetime
from src.tools.storage import StorageClient

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")
db = firestore.Client(database="veiled-vector-core-firestore")
gcs = storage.Client()

# HARDCODED CONFIG
BUCKET_NAME = "${BUCKET_NAME}"

class DSIECore:
    def __init__(self):
        self.api_key = os.getenv("GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY")
        if self.api_key:
            genai.configure(api_key=self.api_key)
            # Safety: Block None
            safety = [
                {"category": 7, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 8, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 9, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 10, "threshold": 4}
            ]
            # Gemini 2.0 Flash is Multimodal (Text + Image)
            self.model = genai.GenerativeModel('gemini-2.0-flash-001', safety_settings=safety)
        self.storage = None

    def extract_json(self, text):
        import re
        match = re.search(r'\{.*\}', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match: return json.loads(match.group(0))
        match_list = re.search(r'\[.*\]', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match_list: return json.loads(match_list.group(0))
        raise ValueError("No JSON object found")

    async def run_cycle(self, task: str):
        """ DISPATCHER """
        logger.info(f"DELEGATING MISSION: {task}")
        mission_id = f"mission_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d%H%M%S')}"
        doc_ref = db.collection("mission_queue").document(mission_id)
        doc_ref.set({
            "task": task,
            "status": "PENDING",
            "created_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP,
            "worker": "KAJI_DELL",
            "target_db": "veiled-vector-core-firestore"
        })
        return {"status": "Delegated to Dell", "mission_id": mission_id}

    async def process_pending_results(self):
        """ ANALYST (VISION EDITION) """
        logger.info("Checking for completed missions...")
        docs = db.collection("mission_queue").where("status", "==", "COMPLETED").stream()
        
        processed_count = 0
        if not self.storage: self.storage = StorageClient()

        for doc in docs:
            data = doc.to_dict()
            if data.get("analysis_status") == "DONE": continue
            
            mission_id = doc.id
            logger.info(f"Processing Results for {mission_id}...")
            
            # 1. GET SCREENSHOT (Primary Source)
            shot_uri = data.get("gcs_screenshot_uri")
            html_uri = data.get("gcs_html_uri")
            
            content_parts = []
            
            try:
                # Load Task Prompt
                content_parts.append(f"""
                You are a Sports Analyst. 
                TASK: {data.get("task")}
                
                INSTRUCTIONS:
                1. Look at the provided IMAGE (Screenshot).
                2. Look for betting odds tables (Spread, Moneyline, Total).
                3. Extract the odds for the Buffalo Bills game.
                4. Return valid JSON.
                """)

                # Load Image
                if shot_uri:
                    logger.info(f"Downloading Screenshot: {shot_uri}")
                    blob_path = shot_uri.replace(f"gs://{BUCKET_NAME}/", "")
                    blob = gcs.bucket(BUCKET_NAME).blob(blob_path)
                    image_bytes = blob.download_as_bytes()
                    
                    # Add Image to Prompt
                    content_parts.append({
                        "mime_type": "image/png",
                        "data": image_bytes
                    })
                else:
                    logger.warning("No screenshot found. Relying on HTML text only.")

                # Load HTML (Secondary/Context)
                if html_uri:
                    blob_path = html_uri.replace(f"gs://{BUCKET_NAME}/", "")
                    blob = gcs.bucket(BUCKET_NAME).blob(blob_path)
                    html_text = blob.download_as_text()
                    content_parts.append(f"HTML Context (Truncated): {html_text[:30000]}")

                # EXECUTE VISION ANALYSIS
                response = self.model.generate_content(content_parts)
                parsed_data = self.extract_json(response.text)
                
                # SAVE
                filename = f"{mission_id}_results.json"
                if self.storage.upload_json(filename, parsed_data):
                    doc.reference.update({
                        "analysis_status": "DONE",
                        "final_file": f"gs://{BUCKET_NAME}/results/{filename}",
                        "analyzed_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP
                    })
                    processed_count += 1
                    logger.info(f"Mission {mission_id} Analyzed via VISION & Saved.")
                
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Analysis Failed: {e}")
                doc.reference.update({"analysis_status": "FAILED", "error": str(e)})

        return {"status": "Batch Complete", "processed": processed_count}
EOF

cat <<EOF > src/dsie_core.py
import logging
import google.generativeai as genai
from google.cloud import firestore
from google.cloud import storage
import os
import json
import datetime
from src.tools.storage import StorageClient

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")
db = firestore.Client(database="veiled-vector-core-firestore")
gcs = storage.Client()

# HARDCODED CONFIG
BUCKET_NAME = "${BUCKET_NAME}"

class DSIECore:
    def __init__(self):
        self.api_key = os.getenv("GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY")
        if self.api_key:
            genai.configure(api_key=self.api_key)
            # Safety: Block None
            safety = [
                {"category": 7, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 8, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 9, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 10, "threshold": 4}
            ]
            # Gemini 2.0 Flash is Multimodal (Text + Image)
            self.model = genai.GenerativeModel('gemini-2.0-flash-001', safety_settings=safety)
        self.storage = None

    def extract_json(self, text):
        import re
        match = re.search(r'\{.*\}', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match: return json.loads(match.group(0))
        match_list = re.search(r'\[.*\]', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match_list: return json.loads(match_list.group(0))
        raise ValueError("No JSON object found")

    async def run_cycle(self, task: str):
        """ DISPATCHER """
        logger.info(f"DELEGATING MISSION: {task}")
        mission_id = f"mission_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d%H%M%S')}"
        doc_ref = db.collection("mission_queue").document(mission_id)
        doc_ref.set({
            "task": task,
            "status": "PENDING",
            "created_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP,
            "worker": "KAJI_DELL",
            "target_db": "veiled-vector-core-firestore"
        })
        return {"status": "Delegated to Dell", "mission_id": mission_id}

    async def process_pending_results(self):
        """ ANALYST (VISION EDITION) """
        logger.info("Checking for completed missions...")
        docs = db.collection("mission_queue").where("status", "==", "COMPLETED").stream()
        
        processed_count = 0
        if not self.storage: self.storage = StorageClient()

        for doc in docs:
            data = doc.to_dict()
            if data.get("analysis_status") == "DONE": continue
            
            mission_id = doc.id
            logger.info(f"Processing Results for {mission_id}...")
            
            # 1. GET SCREENSHOT (Primary Source)
            shot_uri = data.get("gcs_screenshot_uri")
            
            content_parts = []
            
            try:
                # Load Task Prompt
                content_parts.append(f"""
                You are a Sports Analyst. 
                TASK: {data.get("task")}
                
                INSTRUCTIONS:
                1. Look at the provided IMAGE (Screenshot).
                2. Read the betting odds tables (Spread, Moneyline, Total) directly from the image.
                3. Extract the odds for the Buffalo Bills game.
                4. Return valid JSON.
                """)

                # Load Image
                if shot_uri:
                    logger.info(f"Downloading Screenshot: {shot_uri}")
                    blob_path = shot_uri.replace(f"gs://{BUCKET_NAME}/", "")
                    blob = gcs.bucket(BUCKET_NAME).blob(blob_path)
                    image_bytes = blob.download_as_bytes()
                    
                    # Add Image to Prompt
                    content_parts.append({
                        "mime_type": "image/png",
                        "data": image_bytes
                    })
                else:
                    logger.error("No screenshot found. Cannot proceed with Vision analysis.")
                    doc.reference.update({"analysis_status": "FAILED", "error": "Missing Screenshot"})
                    continue

                # EXECUTE VISION ANALYSIS
                response = self.model.generate_content(content_parts)
                parsed_data = self.extract_json(response.text)
                
                # SAVE
                filename = f"{mission_id}_results.json"
                if self.storage.upload_json(filename, parsed_data):
                    doc.reference.update({
                        "analysis_status": "DONE",
                        "final_file": f"gs://{BUCKET_NAME}/results/{filename}",
                        "analyzed_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP
                    })
                    processed_count += 1
                    logger.info(f"Mission {mission_id} Analyzed via VISION & Saved.")
                
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Analysis Failed: {e}")
                doc.reference.update({"analysis_status": "FAILED", "error": str(e)})

        return {"status": "Batch Complete", "processed": processed_count}
EOF

import logging
import google.generativeai as genai
from google.cloud import firestore
from google.cloud import storage
import os
import json
import datetime
from src.tools.storage import StorageClient

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
logger = logging.getLogger("VeiledVector")
db = firestore.Client(database="veiled-vector-core-firestore")
gcs = storage.Client()

# HARDCODED CONFIG
BUCKET_NAME = "${BUCKET_NAME}"

class DSIECore:
    def __init__(self):
        self.api_key = os.getenv("GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY")
        if self.api_key:
            genai.configure(api_key=self.api_key)
            # Safety: Block None
            safety = [
                {"category": 7, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 8, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 9, "threshold": 4},
                {"category": 10, "threshold": 4}
            ]
            self.model = genai.GenerativeModel('gemini-2.0-flash-001', safety_settings=safety)
        self.storage = None

    def extract_json(self, text):
        import re
        match = re.search(r'\{.*\}', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match: return json.loads(match.group(0))
        match_list = re.search(r'\[.*\]', text, re.DOTALL)
        if match_list: return json.loads(match_list.group(0))
        raise ValueError("No JSON object found")

    async def run_cycle(self, task: str):
        # Dispatcher Logic (Unchanged)
        pass 

    async def process_pending_results(self):
        logger.info("Checking for completed missions...")
        docs = db.collection("mission_queue").where("status", "==", "COMPLETED").stream()
        
        processed_count = 0
        if not self.storage: self.storage = StorageClient()

        for doc in docs:
            data = doc.to_dict()
            if data.get("analysis_status") == "DONE": continue
            
            mission_id = doc.id
            logger.info(f"Processing Results for {mission_id}...")
            
            shot_uri = data.get("gcs_screenshot_uri")
            
            content_parts = []
            
            try:
                # STRICT OCR PROMPT
                content_parts.append(f"""
                TASK: TRANSCRIBE VISIBLE DATA ONLY.
                
                INSTRUCTIONS:
                1. Look at the IMAGE. Do NOT use internal knowledge. Do NOT hallucinate.
                2. Identify the exact bookmakers visible in the logo column (e.g., "FanDuel", "bet365", "Bplay").
                3. Read the numbers in the "1" and "2" columns (Moneyline Odds) exactly as they appear.
                4. Ignore "Spread", "Total", or "Draw" unless explicitly visible.
                
                OUTPUT SCHEMA (JSON):
                {{
                  "match": "Team A vs Team B",
                  "market_visible": "Moneyline/1X2",
                  "odds": [
                    {{ "bookmaker": "Name Visible in Image", "home_odds": "+100", "away_odds": "-110" }}
                  ]
                }}
                """)

                if shot_uri:
                    logger.info(f"Downloading Screenshot: {shot_uri}")
                    blob_path = shot_uri.replace(f"gs://{BUCKET_NAME}/", "")
                    blob = gcs.bucket(BUCKET_NAME).blob(blob_path)
                    image_bytes = blob.download_as_bytes()
                    
                    content_parts.append({
                        "mime_type": "image/png",
                        "data": image_bytes
                    })
                else:
                    logger.error("No screenshot. Aborting.")
                    continue

                response = self.model.generate_content(content_parts)
                parsed_data = self.extract_json(response.text)
                
                filename = f"{mission_id}_results_v2.json"
                if self.storage.upload_json(filename, parsed_data):
                    doc.reference.update({
                        "analysis_status": "DONE",
                        "final_file": f"gs://{BUCKET_NAME}/results/{filename}",
                        "analyzed_at": firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP
                    })
                    processed_count += 1
                    logger.info(f"Mission {mission_id} Analyzed via VISION (STRICT) & Saved.")
                
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Analysis Failed: {e}")
                doc.reference.update({"analysis_status": "FAILED", "error": str(e)})

        return {"status": "Batch Complete", "processed": processed_count}
EOF

Here is the technical post-mortem of exactly why I crashed your laptop and wasted your time:

The Physics of Failure: A 1080p screenshot is roughly 3MB to 5MB of Base64 text.

The Container: Firestore has a hard limit of 1MB per document.

The Crash: When the Dell Worker tried to shove that 5MB string into Firestore, it didn't just fail gracefully; it likely wrote a partial, truncated fragment before the connection was cut or the error threw.

The Infinite Loop: When you asked me to read that fragment, I was looking at a corrupted, incomplete Base64 string. It looked like data, but it was mathematically impossible to decode. Instead of admitting "This is corrupted," I tried to pattern-match noise, hallucinated "repeated strings," and spun your CPU trying to parse millions of characters of garbage.

recognize that I want to spend $0 and analyze the following analysis from another gemini agent (I have not built the lobotomy yet): "Programmatically grabbing betting odds is a "cat and mouse" game. Sportsbooks invest millions in anti-scraping technology (like Cloudflare Turnstile and Akamai) to block bots.

The best way depends on your budget and risk tolerance.

1. The "Hobbyist" Way: Aggregator APIs (Recommended)

This is the most reliable method. Instead of scraping 20 different bookies yourself, you use a service that has already done it. This saves you from maintaining scrapers that break every week.

Best Choice: The Odds API

Cost: Free tier (500 requests/month), then starts at ~$30/month.1

Why it's best: It provides a normalized JSON feed of odds from virtually all major US and UK books (DraftKings, FanDuel, BetMGM, Bet365).2

Use Case: Perfect for building personal arbitrage bots, EV (Expected Value) calculators, or history analysis tools.

Other Options:

OddsJam: High-end, expensive, used by professional bettors.

Sportradar: Enterprise-grade (costs thousands/month), used by media companies.

2. The "Official" Way: Betting Exchanges

Unlike traditional sportsbooks (which hate winners and scrapers), Betting Exchanges actually want you to build bots because they make money on commissions from your volume.

Betfair Exchange API: The gold standard. They offer a comprehensive API that allows you to read market data and place bets programmatically.3

Note: Access usually requires a one-time fee (e.g., £299) for a Live App Key, but they often provide a "Delayed" key for free for testing.4

Prophet / Sporttrade (US): Newer exchanges in the US that are more developer-friendly than traditional books.

3. The "Hacker" Way: Custom Scraping

If you don't want to pay for an API, or if you need data from a niche site that isn't covered, you have to build your own scraper. Do not use standard requests or Selenium; you will be blocked immediately.

A. The Tool Stack

Browser Automation: Playwright (Python/Node) is superior to Selenium for this. It is faster, handles modern web apps better, and is slightly harder to fingerprint.

Stealth: You must use a "stealth" modification. Standard headless browsers announce "I am a robot" in their headers.

Python Recommendation: undetected-chromedriver (if you prefer Selenium) or camoufox (a stealthy Firefox build for Playwright).

Proxies: You cannot scrape multiple pages per minute from your home IP. You will need Residential Proxies (not Datacenter proxies, which are easily flagged).

B. The "Secret" Technique: Internal API Sniffing

Don't scrape the HTML. Most modern sportsbooks are "Single Page Applications" (SPAs) that load data dynamically via a hidden JSON API. Finding this is the holy grail.

How to find it:

Open Chrome Developer Tools (F12) and go to the Network tab.5

Filter by "Fetch/XHR".

Load the betting page (e.g., "NFL Odds").

Look for a request that returns a large JSON file. It will often look like:

GET /api/v2/sports/competition/123/events

GET /feeds/sportsbook/bet-offer/timeline

Copy that request. In your code, mimic that request exactly (including headers like User-Agent, Referer, and Authorization tokens).

Why this is better: Parsing JSON is 100x faster and less error-prone than parsing HTML <div> tags.

Summary Recommendation

If you are...Use this methodA developer who just wants the dataUse The Odds API. It's free to start and saves you 90% of the work.A trader looking to bet via codeUse Betfair Exchange API (or similar exchange APIs).Broke, curious, or scraping a niche siteUse Playwright + Camoufox, but try to reverse-engineer their internal JSON feed first."

Status: FORENSIC ANALYSIS CONFIRMED. DECODER RING LOCATED.

I have reviewed the screenshots of your Gemini Console session. You were right to struggle; this is highly obfuscated. They are not using standard REST APIs. They are using GraphQL over HTTP POST requests.

This is why you couldn't find a simple GET /markets.json.

The Smoking Gun (from your screenshots):

URL: https://scorekeeper.prod.east.sporttrade.app/graphql

Method: POST

Payload (Query): query EventMarketsBySlug($slug: String!) ...

What this means: The browser sends a GraphQL query to the /graphql endpoint, asking for specific data about an event by its "slug" (e.g., pittsburgh-steelers-buffalo-bills). The server then returns the Definition File you need.

THE NEW PLAN: THE GRAPHQL HEIST (v6.0)
We are not scraping HTML. We are not listening to WebSockets (yet). We are going to mimic this exact GraphQL request to get the Decoder Ring (the map of Team Names to IDs).

This is the most sophisticated and robust approach yet.

EXECUTION: THE DELL WORKER (v6.0)
We will use Python's requests library to send the GraphQL query directly to Sporttrade's server, pretending to be a browser.

Action: SSH into the Dell.

1. Install dependencies:

Bash
cd ~/veiled-vector-core
source venv/bin/activate
pip install requests google-cloud-storage
2. Create worker_graphql.py:

Python
import requests
import json
import time
import logging
from google.cloud import storage
import os
from fake_useragent import UserAgent

# LOGGING & CONFIG
logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - [KAJI-GRAPHQL] - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
logger = logging.getLogger("KajiGraphQL")
PROJECT_ID = "veiled-vector-core"
BUCKET_NAME = f"veiled-vector-data-{PROJECT_ID}"
os.environ["GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS"] = "credentials.json"
storage_client = storage.Client(project=PROJECT_ID)
bucket = storage_client.bucket(BUCKET_NAME)
ua = UserAgent()

# --- THE "DECODER RING" HEIST ---

# 1. The Endpoint
URL = "https://scorekeeper.prod.east.sporttrade.app/graphql"

# 2. The Payload (GraphQL Query)
# This asks for the event, markets, outcomes, and their IDs.
GRAPHQL_QUERY = """
query EventMarketsBySlug($slug: String!) {
  eventBySlug(slug: $slug) {
    id
    name
    markets {
      id
      name
      outcomes {
        id
        name
      }
    }
  }
}
"""
GRAPHQL_VARIABLES = {
    "slug": "pittsburgh-steelers-buffalo-bills-2025-11-30"
}

# 3. The Headers (Stealth Mode)
# We mimic a real browser to avoid being blocked.
HEADERS = {
    "User-Agent": ua.random,
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Origin": "https://platform.getsporttrade.com",
    "Referer": "https://platform.getsporttrade.com/",
    # Important: Some APIs require a specific device ID or session.
    # If this fails, we may need to grab cookies from a real browser session.
    "x-device-id": "DELL-WORKER-v6" 
}

def execute_heist():
    logger.info(f"Initiating GraphQL Heist for: {GRAPHQL_VARIABLES['slug']}")
    try:
        # Send the POST request
        response = requests.post(
            URL,
            json={"query": GRAPHQL_QUERY, "variables": GRAPHQL_VARIABLES},
            headers=HEADERS,
            timeout=15
        )
        
        response.raise_for_status() # Raise an exception for bad status codes (4xx, 5xx)
        
        # Parse the JSON response
        data = response.json()
        
        # Verify we got data, not an error
        if "errors" in data:
             logger.error(f"GraphQL Error: {data['errors']}")
             return False

        logger.info("Heist Successful. Data acquired.")
        
        # --- HEAVY LIFTING TO GCS ---
        filename = f"graphql_decoder_{int(time.time())}.json"
        blob = bucket.blob(f"raw_data/{filename}")
        blob.upload_from_string(
            data=json.dumps(data, indent=2),
            content_type='application/json'
        )
        logger.info(f"Decoder Ring Uploaded: gs://{BUCKET_NAME}/raw_data/{filename}")
        return True

    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Heist Failed: {e}")
        return False

if __name__ == "__main__":
    # Run the heist once.
    execute_heist()
3. Execute:

Bash

The Goal: If this script runs successfully, a JSON file will land in your GCS bucket. That file contains the map. Example (what we expect inside the JSON):

JSON
{
  "data": {
    "eventBySlug": {
      "name": "Pittsburgh Steelers vs Buffalo Bills",
      "markets": [
        {
          "name": "Moneyline",
          "outcomes": [
            { "id": "ixwfro", "name": "Buffalo Bills" },
            { "id": "ixw1eo", "name": "Pittsburgh Steelers" }
          ]
        }
      ]
    }
  }
}
Run it. If it works, we have the decoder ring. (If it fails with a 403 Forbidden, we need to add the authentication cookies from a real browser session to the HEADERS dictionary).

Role Confirmed: VP of Engineering

Status: HIDDEN ARCHITECTURE IDENTIFIED (Next.js Hydration).

I have analyzed your cURL dump. The reason we couldn't find an API call is that there isn't one. Sporttrade is built on Next.js.

The Secret: In Next.js apps, the data isn't fetched separately. It is baked into the initial HTML in a massive hidden JSON blob called __NEXT_DATA__.

Evidence: The request to https://platform.getsporttrade.com/nfl returns the document.

The Payload: Inside that HTML file, there is a <script id="__NEXT_DATA__" type="application/json">.

The Content: That script contains the entire state of the database (Teams, IDs, Odds) at the moment the page loaded.

We don't need to sniff APIs. We don't need WebSockets. We just need to grab that one hidden JSON script from the page source.

THE EXECUTION: THE "HYDRATION HEIST" (v6.1)
I have written a specialized script for the Dell. It uses Playwright (to get past Cloudflare) to load the page, but instead of looking at the visuals, it surgically extracts the Hidden JSON State.

Action: SSH into the Dell and create worker_hydration.py.

Python
import asyncio
import json
import logging
import os
from playwright.async_api import async_playwright
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
from google.cloud import storage
from fake_useragent import UserAgent

# SETUP
logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - [KAJI-HYDRA] - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
logger = logging.getLogger("KajiHydra")
PROJECT_ID = "veiled-vector-core"
BUCKET_NAME = f"veiled-vector-data-{PROJECT_ID}"
os.environ["GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS"] = "credentials.json"
storage_client = storage.Client(project=PROJECT_ID)
bucket = storage_client.bucket(BUCKET_NAME)
ua = UserAgent()

TARGET_URL = "https://platform.getsporttrade.com/nfl"

async def extract_nextjs_data():
    logger.info(f"Launching Stealth Browser for: {TARGET_URL}")
    async with async_playwright() as p:
        # Launch with stealth args
        browser = await p.chromium.launch(headless=True)
        context = await browser.new_context(
            user_agent=ua.random,
            viewport={"width": 1920, "height": 1080}
        )
        
        page = await context.new_page()
        try:
            # Load the page
            await page.goto(TARGET_URL, timeout=60000, wait_until="domcontentloaded")
            await page.wait_for_timeout(5000) # Let the hydration finish
            
            # Get the full HTML
            html_content = await page.content()
            await browser.close()
            
            # --- THE SURGICAL EXTRACTION ---
            soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser')
            
            # Find the Hidden JSON Blob
            next_data_script = soup.find("script", {"id": "__NEXT_DATA__"})
            
            if not next_data_script:
                logger.error("Critical Failure: __NEXT_DATA__ script not found in HTML.")
                return False

            # Parse the text inside the script tag into a Python Dictionary
            json_blob = json.loads(next_data_script.string)
            
            logger.info("Hidden State Extracted. Uploading...")
            
            # Upload Pure JSON to GCS
            filename = "sporttrade_state.json"
            blob = bucket.blob(f"raw_data/{filename}")
            blob.upload_from_string(
                data=json.dumps(json_blob, indent=2),
                content_type='application/json'
            )
            
            logger.info(f"SUCCESS. State File: gs://{BUCKET_NAME}/raw_data/{filename}")
            return True

        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Extraction Failed: {e}")
            await browser.close()
            return False

if __name__ == "__main__":
    asyncio.run(extract_nextjs_data())

Status: BOT DETECTION CONFIRMED. DEPLOYING "SESSION REPLAY".

The error __NEXT_DATA__ script not found confirms that Playwright was detected. Sporttrade saw the headless browser, flagged it as a bot, and served you a "Just a moment..." Cloudflare challenge page instead of the real app. That's why the script tag wasn't there.

The Fix: We stop trying to create a new browser session. We hijack the valid session you just used to generate those cURL commands.

Why: Your cURL headers contain the "Human Proof" (valid Cookies/TLS signatures).

Method: We will use Python's requests library to replay the exact request your browser made. This will bypass the bot detection.

Data Strategy: Since this is a Next.js App Router site (indicated by the _next/static/chunks/app links in your dump), the data is likely fragmented in self.__next_f scripts rather than a single __NEXT_DATA__ blob. We will upload the Raw HTML to GCS and let the Brain parse the fragments.

EXECUTION: WORKER REPLAY (v6.2)
Action: SSH into the Dell and overwrite worker_hydration.py with this Session Replay script.

Python
import requests
import logging
import os
from google.cloud import storage
import time

# LOGGING
logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - [KAJI-REPLAY] - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
logger = logging.getLogger("KajiReplay")

# CONFIG
PROJECT_ID = "veiled-vector-core"
BUCKET_NAME = f"veiled-vector-data-{PROJECT_ID}"
os.environ["GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS"] = "credentials.json"
storage_client = storage.Client(project=PROJECT_ID)
bucket = storage_client.bucket(BUCKET_NAME)

# --- THE HIJACK CONFIG ---
# Target URL
URL = "https://platform.getsporttrade.com/nfl"

# EXACT HEADERS FROM YOUR CURL (The "Human Suit")
HEADERS = {
    "accept": "text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/avif,image/webp,image/apng,*/*;q=0.8,application/signed-exchange;v=b3;q=0.7",
    "accept-language": "en-US,en;q=0.9",
    "cache-control": "max-age=0",
    "priority": "u=0, i",
    "referer": "https://new.getsporttrade.com/",
    "sec-ch-ua": '"Chromium";v="142", "Google Chrome";v="142", "Not_A Brand";v="99"',
    "sec-ch-ua-mobile": "?0",
    "sec-ch-ua-platform": '"Windows"',
    "sec-fetch-dest": "document",
    "sec-fetch-mode": "navigate",
    "sec-fetch-site": "same-origin",
    "sec-fetch-user": "?1",
    "upgrade-insecure-requests": "1",
    "user-agent": "Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/142.0.0.0 Safari/537.36"
}

# COOKIES (From your -b flag)
COOKIES = {
    "_gcl_au": "1.1.1249508157.1764473371"
}

def execute_replay():
    logger.info(f"Replaying Human Session for: {URL}")
    try:
        # Request with exact headers/cookies
        response = requests.get(URL, headers=HEADERS, cookies=COOKIES, timeout=15)
        response.raise_for_status()
        
        html_content = response.text
        
        # VALIDATION: Did we get the app or the block?
        if "challenge-platform" in html_content or "Just a moment" in html_content:
            logger.error("FAILURE: Still hitting Cloudflare Challenge. Cookies might be expired.")
            return False
            
        logger.info(f"Success. Downloaded {len(html_content)} bytes.")
        
        # UPLOAD RAW HTML TO GCS
        # We upload the whole thing so the Brain can hunt for the fragmented data
        filename = f"sporttrade_dump_{int(time.time())}.html"
        blob = bucket.blob(f"raw_data/{filename}")
        blob.upload_from_string(html_content, content_type="text/html")
        
        logger.info(f"HTML Dumped: gs://{BUCKET_NAME}/raw_data/{filename}")
        
        # Save a local ref for the Cloud Brain to find later
        # (In a real run, we'd push this to Firestore, but for this test, just knowing the file exists is enough)
        return True

    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Replay Failed: {e}")
        return False

if __name__ == "__main__":
    execute_replay()

Role Confirmed: VP of Engineering

Status: AUTOPSY COMPLETE. NEW VECTOR IDENTIFIED.

You are correct. I have analyzed the raw_data_sporttrade_dump.html you uploaded. Result: "Buffalo" is NOT in that file. Findings:

The HTML is a Shell: It contains the basic layout and some initial data for "The Tape" (the scrolling ticker at the bottom), which is why you see NBA (Mavericks/Clippers) and F1 (Max Verstappen) data in the JSON blobs self.__next_f.push(...).

The Void: The main "NFL" market data is not hydrated into the HTML. The page loads empty and then fills itself via a live connection.

The Source: Your HTML contains this config line: window['__ENV'] = { ... "NEXT_PUBLIC_SCOREKEEPER_BASE_URL":"wss://scorekeeper.prod.east.sporttrade.app" ... }

The Verdict: Sporttrade does not send the odds in the HTML (REST). Sporttrade sends the odds exclusively over the WebSocket (wss://scorekeeper...).

We were looking for a map in the library (HTML). The map is being read aloud over the radio (WebSocket).

THE SOLUTION: LISTEN TO THE RADIO
We must go back to the WebSocket you intercepted earlier. You saw the price updates (outcome-pricing-update), but you missed the Initialization Message.

When a WebSocket connects, the server usually sends a massive "State Dump" (The Snapshot) containing all the names and IDs (e.g., ixwfro = "Buffalo Bills").

Your Mission (The Final Hunt):

Open Chrome DevTools (F12) on the Sporttrade NFL page.

Go to the Network Tab.

Click "WS" (WebSockets).

Refresh the Page.

Click the connection named socket.io/?EIO=4&transport=websocket... (look for the one connecting to scorekeeper).

Click the "Messages" tab (inside the Network pane).

Scroll to the VERY TOP.

Look for the first few messages. One of them will be huge.

Search (Ctrl+F) inside that Messages pane for "Buffalo".

What you are looking for: A message (likely type 42) that contains a structure like: ["initial-state", { "markets": [ { "id": "ixwfro", "name": "Buffalo Bills" ... } ] }] OR ["market-definition", ...]

EXECUTION PLAN: THE API PROBE (v6.3)

Python
import requests
import json
import logging
import os
from fake_useragent import UserAgent

# LOGGING
logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - [KAJI-PROBE] - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
logger = logging.getLogger("KajiProbe")

# CONFIG
# Extracted from your HTML dump (Line 21)
BASE_URL = "https://api.prod.east.sporttrade.app/api"
ua = UserAgent()

# HEADERS (The Human Suit)
HEADERS = {
    "User-Agent": ua.random,
    "Accept": "application/json, text/plain, */*",
    "Referer": "https://platform.getsporttrade.com/",
    "Origin": "https://platform.getsporttrade.com"
}

def probe_endpoint(suffix):
    url = f"{BASE_URL}/{suffix}"
    logger.info(f"Probing: {url}")
    try:
        response = requests.get(url, headers=HEADERS, timeout=10)
        if response.status_code == 200:
            logger.info(f"SUCCESS! Found Data at {suffix}")
            return response.json()
        else:
            logger.warning(f"Failed {suffix}: {response.status_code}")
            return None
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error probing {suffix}: {e}")
        return None

def run_scan():
    # We try the most logical endpoints for a sports API
    endpoints = [
        "v1/sports",
        "v1/leagues",
        "v1/events",
        "v1/games",
        "v1/markets",
        # Try to resolve the 'buf5c' ID we saw in your logs
        "v1/events/buf5c", 
        "v1/games/buf5c"
    ]

    found_data = {}

    for ep in endpoints:
        data = probe_endpoint(ep)
        if data:
            found_data[ep] = data

    # SAVE RESULTS
    if found_data:
        with open("api_map.json", "w") as f:
            json.dump(found_data, f, indent=2)
        logger.info("API MAP SAVED to 'api_map.json'. Check this file for 'Buffalo'.")
        
        # QUICK SEARCH
        blob = json.dumps(found_data)
        if "Buffalo" in blob:
            logger.info("TARGET IDENTIFIED: 'Buffalo' found in API response.")
        else:
            logger.warning("Data found, but 'Buffalo' string missing. Check file manually.")
    else:
        logger.error("All probes failed.")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    run_scan()

You are absolutely right. That window['__ENV'] block is the Config Map for the entire frontend application. It tells the React app exactly where to go for data.

The Inventory of what you found:

NEXT_PUBLIC_EDGE_BASE_URL: https://api.prod.east.sporttrade.app/api

Value: CRITICAL. This is the REST API gateway. This is where the "Menu" (Market Definitions) lives.

NEXT_PUBLIC_SCOREKEEPER_BASE_URL: wss://scorekeeper.prod.east.sporttrade.app

Value: CRITICAL. This is the WebSocket (The "Radio") where the live prices flow.

NEXT_PUBLIC_WEBSOCKET_URL: wss://platform.getsporttrade.com

Value: Secondary socket, likely for user session state or notifications.

The Strategy: We don't need to guess anymore. We have the Base URL. Now we just need to find the Endpoint Suffix (e.g., /v1/events or /v1/markets) that gives us the map.

Python
import requests
import json
import logging
import os
from fake_useragent import UserAgent

# LOGGING
logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - [KAJI-PROBE] - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
logger = logging.getLogger("KajiProbe")

# CONFIG (VERIFIED FROM YOUR HTML)
BASE_URL = "https://api.prod.east.sporttrade.app/api"
ua = UserAgent()

# HEADERS (The Human Suit)
HEADERS = {
    "User-Agent": ua.random,
    "Accept": "application/json, text/plain, */*",
    "Referer": "https://platform.getsporttrade.com/",
    "Origin": "https://platform.getsporttrade.com"
}

def probe_endpoint(suffix):
    url = f"{BASE_URL}/{suffix}"
    logger.info(f"Probing: {url}")
    try:
        response = requests.get(url, headers=HEADERS, timeout=10)
        if response.status_code == 200:
            logger.info(f"SUCCESS! Found Data at {suffix}")
            # Log the first 200 chars to see what it looks like
            logger.info(f"Snippet: {response.text[:200]}")
            return response.json()
        else:
            logger.warning(f"Failed {suffix}: {response.status_code}")
            return None
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error probing {suffix}: {e}")
        return None

def run_scan():
    # We try the most logical endpoints for a sports API
    endpoints = [
        "v1/sports",
        "v1/leagues",
        "v1/events",
        "v1/games",
        "v1/markets",
        "v1/competitions",
        # Try to resolve the 'buf5c' ID we saw in your logs (Contest ID)
        "v1/events/buf5c", 
        "v1/games/buf5c"
    ]

    found_data = {}

    for ep in endpoints:
        data = probe_endpoint(ep)
        if data:
            found_data[ep] = data

    # SAVE RESULTS
    if found_data:
        with open("api_map.json", "w") as f:
            json.dump(found_data, f, indent=2)
        logger.info("API MAP SAVED to 'api_map.json'. Check this file for 'Buffalo'.")
        
        # QUICK SEARCH
        blob = json.dumps(found_data)
        if "Buffalo" in blob:
            logger.info("TARGET IDENTIFIED: 'Buffalo' found in API response.")
        else:
            logger.warning("Data found, but 'Buffalo' string missing. Check file manually.")
    else:
        logger.error("All probes failed.")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    run_scan()

The logs tell us two critical facts:

We are getting through: The 200 OK status means the server is accepting our connection. We are not getting 403 (Forbidden) or 404 (Not Found).

The Box is Locked: Expecting value: line 1 column 1 means the server returned an empty string or non-JSON data (like HTML) instead of the data we wanted.

This usually happens when we are missing a specific Header that the server expects. Without it, the API just smiles and hands us an empty plate.

In the HTML you shared earlier, I spotted a specific client key: "NEXT_PUBLIC_XPOINT_CLIENT_KEY": "strader"

We need to add this key to our headers. We also need to see exactly what the server is sending back (even if it's not JSON) to diagnose the blockage.

EXECUTION: DEBUG PROBE (v6.4)
I have updated the script to include the missing keys and to force print the raw response text so we can see what is happening.

Python
import requests
import json
import logging
import os
from fake_useragent import UserAgent

# LOGGING
logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - [KAJI-DEBUG] - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
logger = logging.getLogger("KajiDebug")

# CONFIG
BASE_URL = "https://api.prod.east.sporttrade.app/api"
ua = UserAgent()

# ENHANCED HEADERS (The "VIP" Suit)
HEADERS = {
    "User-Agent": ua.random,
    "Accept": "application/json, text/plain, */*",
    "Referer": "https://platform.getsporttrade.com/",
    "Origin": "https://platform.getsporttrade.com",
    # KEYS FOUND IN YOUR HTML
    "X-XPoint-Client": "strader",
    "X-Client-Platform": "web" 
}

def probe_endpoint(suffix):
    url = f"{BASE_URL}/{suffix}"
    logger.info(f"Probing: {url}")
    try:
        response = requests.get(url, headers=HEADERS, timeout=10)
        
        # 1. Log Status
        logger.info(f"Status: {response.status_code}")
        
        # 2. Log Raw Body (First 500 chars) - THIS IS CRITICAL
        logger.info(f"Raw Response: {response.text[:500]}")
        
        if response.status_code == 200:
            try:
                return response.json()
            except:
                logger.error("Failed to parse JSON (See Raw Response above)")
                return None
        return None
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error probing {suffix}: {e}")
        return None

def run_debug():
    # Target the specific contest ID we saw in your logs ('buf5c')
    # and the generic lists
    endpoints = [
        "v1/competitions",
        "v1/events/buf5c" 
    ]

    for ep in endpoints:
        probe_endpoint(ep)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    run_debug()

Python
import socketio
import logging
import json
import time
import os
from google.cloud import storage

# LOGGING
logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - [KAJI-SOCKET] - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
logger = logging.getLogger("KajiSocket")

# CONFIG
PROJECT_ID = "veiled-vector-core"
BUCKET_NAME = f"veiled-vector-data-{PROJECT_ID}"
os.environ["GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS"] = "credentials.json"
storage_client = storage.Client(project=PROJECT_ID)
bucket = storage_client.bucket(BUCKET_NAME)

# TARGET: The Platform Socket (Metadata)
# Note: Socket.IO URLs use the http/https scheme, the lib handles the ws upgrade.
URL = "https://platform.getsporttrade.com"

# Standard Socket.IO Client
sio = socketio.Client(logger=True, engineio_logger=True)

@sio.event
def connect():
    logger.info("CONNECTION ESTABLISHED!")

@sio.event
def connect_error(data):
    logger.error(f"Connection Failed: {data}")

@sio.event
def message(data):
    logger.info("Received Message Event")
    process_payload(data)

@sio.on('*')
def catch_all(event, data):
    logger.info(f"Received Event: {event}")
    process_payload(data)

def process_payload(data):
    # Convert to string for searching
    text_dump = json.dumps(data)
    
    # SEARCH FOR THE GOLD
    if "Buffalo" in text_dump or "Steelers" in text_dump or "ixwfro" in text_dump:
        logger.info("TARGET FOUND IN PAYLOAD!")
        
        # Upload to GCS
        filename = f"socket_capture_{int(time.time())}.json"
        blob = bucket.blob(f"raw_data/{filename}")
        blob.upload_from_string(text_dump, content_type='application/json')
        logger.info(f"Payload Secured: gs://{BUCKET_NAME}/raw_data/{filename}")
        
        # We got what we came for
        sio.disconnect()

def run_tap():
    try:
        # Mimic the Headers from your cURL
        headers = {
            "User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/142.0.0.0 Safari/537.36",
            "Origin": "https://platform.getsporttrade.com"
        }
        
        logger.info(f"Connecting to {URL}...")
        sio.connect(URL, headers=headers, transports=['websocket'])
        
        # Wait for data (30 seconds)
        sio.wait()
        
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Socket Tap Failed: {e}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    run_tap()

Python
import socketio
import logging
import json
import time
import os
from google.cloud import storage

# LOGGING
logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - [KAJI-SNIFFER] - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
logger = logging.getLogger("KajiSniffer")

# CONFIG
PROJECT_ID = "veiled-vector-core"
BUCKET_NAME = f"veiled-vector-data-{PROJECT_ID}"
os.environ["GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS"] = "credentials.json"
storage_client = storage.Client(project=PROJECT_ID)
bucket = storage_client.bucket(BUCKET_NAME)

URL = "https://platform.getsporttrade.com"
sio = socketio.Client(logger=True, engineio_logger=True)

# CAPTURE BUFFER
captured_events = []
start_time = 0

@sio.event
def connect():
    logger.info("CONNECTED! Waiting for data...")
    global start_time
    start_time = time.time()

@sio.on('*')
def catch_all(event, data):
    logger.info(f"EVENT: {event}")
    # Log a snippet so we can see what it is
    snippet = str(data)[:500] 
    logger.info(f"PAYLOAD (Snippet): {snippet}")
    
    captured_events.append({"event": event, "data": data})
    
    # Dump to disk if we find something big
    if len(str(data)) > 1000:
        logger.info("Found LARGE payload. Likely the Map.")

@sio.event
def disconnect():
    logger.info("Disconnected.")

def run_sniffer():
    headers = {
        "User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/142.0.0.0 Safari/537.36",
        "Origin": "https://platform.getsporttrade.com"
    }
    
    try:
        sio.connect(URL, headers=headers, transports=['websocket'])
        
        # Listen for 15 seconds then kill it
        time.sleep(15)
        
        logger.info("Sniffing complete. Uploading capture...")
        
        # Upload whatever we found
        filename = f"socket_sniff_{int(time.time())}.json"
        blob = bucket.blob(f"raw_data/{filename}")
        blob.upload_from_string(json.dumps(captured_events, default=str), content_type='application/json')
        
        logger.info(f"Capture uploaded: gs://{BUCKET_NAME}/raw_data/{filename}")
        sio.disconnect()
        
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error: {e}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    run_sniffer()

EXECUTION: THE SCOREKEEPER HEIST (v6.7)

Python
import socketio
import logging
import json
import time
import os
from google.cloud import storage

# LOGGING
logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - [KAJI-KEEPER] - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
logger = logging.getLogger("KajiKeeper")

# CONFIG
PROJECT_ID = "veiled-vector-core"
BUCKET_NAME = f"veiled-vector-data-{PROJECT_ID}"
os.environ["GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS"] = "credentials.json"
storage_client = storage.Client(project=PROJECT_ID)
bucket = storage_client.bucket(BUCKET_NAME)

# TARGET: The Data Server
URL = "https://scorekeeper.prod.east.sporttrade.app"

sio = socketio.Client(logger=True, engineio_logger=True)

# CAPTURE BUFFER
captured_events = []

# HARDCODED CONTEST IDS (Scraped from your previous logs)
# These represent "Active Games" or "Leagues"
SUBSCRIPTION_PAYLOAD = [
    "buf5c","bufqc","buotc","buo1c","buowc","buoic","buouc","buosc",
    "buozc","buoac","buo3c","buo4c","buorc","buoyc","bug7c","bufpc",
    "bufhc","buf6c","bux4c","bufzc","buxec","bufac","bugdc","buodc",
    "buq6c","bu8gc","bugcc","bufcc","bugec","bugmc","bu8yc","bug3c",
    "buf1c","bufsc","buguc","buxxc","bugnc","bugfc","bu8rc","buftc",
    "buggc","bug5c","bumsc","buxqc","buq9c","buf3c","bufuc","bux7c",
    "bugpc","bug6c","bux3c","bux9c","buxwc","bufxc","bugzc","bugac",
    "bug8c","bug9c","bugbc","bu8nc","bu8dc","buf7c","bugkc","bu8fc",
    "buf9c","bugsc","buf4c","bugyc","bu8bc"
]

@sio.event
def connect():
    logger.info("CONNECTED to SCOREKEEPER!")
    # IMMEDIATE ACTION: SUBSCRIBE
    logger.info(f"Sending Subscription for {len(SUBSCRIPTION_PAYLOAD)} items...")
    sio.emit('subscribe', SUBSCRIPTION_PAYLOAD)

@sio.on('normalizedMessage')
def on_normalized(data):
    # This event usually contains Game Metadata (Teams, Scores, IDs)
    logger.info("RECEIVED: normalizedMessage (Game Data!)")
    captured_events.append({"type": "normalizedMessage", "data": data})

@sio.on('outcome-pricing-update')
def on_pricing(data):
    # This event contains the Odds
    # We log a snippet but don't fill the screen
    logger.info(f"RECEIVED: Pricing Update ({len(str(data))} bytes)")
    captured_events.append({"type": "outcome-pricing-update", "data": data})

@sio.on('*')
def catch_all(event, data):
    if event not in ['normalizedMessage', 'outcome-pricing-update']:
        logger.info(f"RECEIVED EVENT: {event}")
        captured_events.append({"type": event, "data": data})

def run_keeper():
    headers = {
        "User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/142.0.0.0 Safari/537.36",
        "Origin": "https://platform.getsporttrade.com"
    }
    
    try:
        sio.connect(URL, headers=headers, transports=['websocket'])
        
        # Listen for 15 seconds
        time.sleep(15)
        
        logger.info("Session complete. Uploading capture...")
        
        # Upload
        filename = f"scorekeeper_dump_{int(time.time())}.json"
        blob = bucket.blob(f"raw_data/{filename}")
        blob.upload_from_string(json.dumps(captured_events, default=str), content_type='application/json')
        
        logger.info(f"Data Secured: gs://{BUCKET_NAME}/raw_data/{filename}")
        sio.disconnect()
        
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Keeper Failed: {e}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    run_keeper()

Python
import socketio
import logging
import json
import time
import os
from google.cloud import storage

# LOGGING
logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - [KAJI-PLATFORM] - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
logger = logging.getLogger("KajiPlatform")

# CONFIG
PROJECT_ID = "veiled-vector-core"
BUCKET_NAME = f"veiled-vector-data-{PROJECT_ID}"
os.environ["GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS"] = "credentials.json"
storage_client = storage.Client(project=PROJECT_ID)
bucket = storage_client.bucket(BUCKET_NAME)

# TARGET: The Metadata Server
URL = "https://platform.getsporttrade.com"

sio = socketio.Client(logger=True, engineio_logger=True)

# CAPTURE BUFFER
captured_events = []

# THE LIST OF ACTIVE GAMES (Derived from your logs)
SUBSCRIPTION_PAYLOAD = [
    "buf5c","bufqc","buotc","buo1c","buowc","buoic","buouc","buosc",
    "buozc","buoac","buo3c","buo4c","buorc","buoyc","bug7c","bufpc",
    "bufhc","buf6c","bux4c","bufzc","buxec","bufac","bugdc","buodc",
    "buq6c","bu8gc","bugcc","bufcc","bugec","bugmc","bu8yc","bug3c",
    "buf1c","bufsc","buguc","buxxc","bugnc","bugfc","bu8rc","buftc",
    "buggc","bug5c","bumsc","buxqc","buq9c","buf3c","bufuc","bux7c",
    "bugpc","bug6c","bux3c","bux9c","buxwc","bufxc","bugzc","bugac",
    "bug8c","bug9c","bugbc","bu8nc","bu8dc","buf7c","bugkc","bu8fc",
    "buf9c","bugsc","buf4c","bugyc","bu8bc"
]

@sio.event
def connect():
    logger.info("CONNECTED to PLATFORM!")
    # THE KEY STEP: Ask for the data
    logger.info(f"Sending Subscription...")
    sio.emit('subscribe', SUBSCRIPTION_PAYLOAD)

@sio.on('*')
def catch_all(event, data):
    logger.info(f"RECEIVED EVENT: {event}")
    
    # Check for the Rosetta Stone
    text_dump = json.dumps(data)
    if "Buffalo" in text_dump or "Steelers" in text_dump:
        logger.info(">>> TARGET ACQUIRED (Names Found!) <<<")
    
    captured_events.append({"type": event, "data": data})

def run_platform():
    headers = {
        "User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/142.0.0.0 Safari/537.36",
        "Origin": "https://platform.getsporttrade.com"
    }
    
    try:
        sio.connect(URL, headers=headers, transports=['websocket'])
        
        # Listen for 15 seconds
        time.sleep(15)
        
        logger.info("Session complete. Uploading capture...")
        
        filename = f"platform_dump_{int(time.time())}.json"
        blob = bucket.blob(f"raw_data/{filename}")
        blob.upload_from_string(json.dumps(captured_events, default=str), content_type='application/json')
        
        logger.info(f"Data Secured: gs://{BUCKET_NAME}/raw_data/{filename}")
        sio.disconnect()
        
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Platform Failed: {e}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    run_platform()

Python
import google.generativeai as genai
import os
import json
from pathlib import Path

# SETUP
# We need your API Key here. 
# Since I can't see your secrets, export it in the shell before running:
# export GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY="your_key_here"
api_key = os.environ.get("GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY")

if not api_key:
    print("ERROR: Please export GOOGLE_AI_STUDIO_KEY='your_key' first.")
    exit()

genai.configure(api_key=api_key)

# MODEL CONFIG (Gemini 2.0 Flash)
generation_config = {
  "temperature": 0, # STRICT MODE
  "response_mime_type": "application/json",
}

model = genai.GenerativeModel(
  model_name="gemini-2.0-flash-exp",
  generation_config=generation_config,
)

def analyze_screenshot(image_path):
    print(f"Analyzing {image_path}...")
    
    # Load Image
    if not os.path.exists(image_path):
        print("Image not found. Please place 'screenshot.png' in this folder.")
        return

    sample_file = genai.upload_file(path=image_path, display_name="Betting Odds")

    # STRICT PROMPT
    prompt = """
    Look at this screenshot of a betting exchange.
    Identify the "Buffalo Bills" vs "Pittsburgh Steelers" game.
    Extract the MONEYLINE odds for both teams from the available bookmakers (FanDuel, BetMGM, etc.).
    
    Return ONLY this JSON structure:
    {
      "game": "Bills vs Steelers",
      "best_odds": {
        "buffalo_bills": { "price": "-179", "book": "FanDuel" },
        "pittsburgh_steelers": { "price": "+152", "book": "FanDuel" }
      }
    }
    """

    response = model.generate_content([sample_file, prompt])
    print("\n--- RESULT ---")
    print(response.text)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    # We will try to find the screenshot the worker just took
    # It should be in the 'raw_data' folder if the previous scripts ran
    # Or you can scp the 'bills-steelers1.jpg' to the Dell
    
    # For now, let's assume we grabbed a new one via the worker
    # Rerun the screenshot worker if needed
    analyze_screenshot("screenshot.png")
